### `customer/js/place_order.js`

This is the most complex customer JS file. Full implementation required.

```javascript
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {

  // State
  let allItems = [];        // All inventory items loaded
  let selectedItems = {};   // { inventory_id: { ...itemData, quantity: X } }
  let currentPage = 1;
  const itemsPerPage = 20;  // ORDER_ITEMS_PER_PAGE
  const deliveryFee = parseFloat('{PHP_DELIVERY_FEE}'); // Injected by PHP
  let reorderItems = null;  // Pre-selected items from reorder (injected by PHP if applicable)

  // Load items on page load
  loadItems();

  // Check for reorder data (PHP can output a JS variable)
  // e.g., const reorderData = <?php echo json_encode($reorder_items ?? null); ?>;
  // If reorderData exists, pre-select those items after loading

  function loadItems(search = '') {
    showLoading();
    const params = { status_filter: 'active', page: currentPage, search: search };
    ajaxGet('/api/inventory/get_items.php', params)
      .then(data => {
        allItems = data.items;
        renderItems(data.items);
        renderPagination(data.total, data.page, data.per_page);
        hideLoading();

        // If reorder, pre-select matching items
        if (reorderData && currentPage === 1) {
          preselectReorderItems(reorderData);
          reorderData = null; // Only do this once
        }
      })
      .catch(err => {
        showToast('Failed to load items', 'error');
        hideLoading();
      });
  }

  function renderItems(items) {
    const grid = document.getElementById('itemsGrid');
    // Clear existing items (keep spinner)
    grid.querySelectorAll('.item-card').forEach(c => c.remove());

    items.forEach(item => {
      const isSelected = selectedItems[item.id] !== undefined;
      const isOutOfStock = item.stock_count <= 0 || item.status === 'out_of_stock';
      const quantity = isSelected ? selectedItems[item.id].quantity : 1;

      const card = document.createElement('div');
      card.className = `item-card ${isSelected ? 'selected' : ''} ${isOutOfStock ? 'out-of-stock' : ''}`;
      card.dataset.itemId = item.id;
      card.innerHTML = `
        <div class="item-card-check"><span class="material-icons">check_circle</span></div>
        ${isOutOfStock ? '<div class="out-of-stock-overlay">Out of Stock</div>' : ''}
        <img src="${item.item_icon || '/assets/images/default-item.png'}" class="item-card-icon" alt="${item.item_name}">
        <div class="item-card-name">${item.item_name}</div>
        <div class="item-card-price">₱${parseFloat(item.price).toFixed(2)}</div>
        <div class="item-card-stock ${item.stock_count <= 10 ? 'low-stock' : ''}">
          ${item.stock_count} in stock
        </div>
        <div class="qty-control">
          <button class="qty-btn qty-minus" data-item-id="${item.id}" ${quantity <= 1 ? 'disabled' : ''}>
            <span class="material-icons">remove</span>
          </button>
          <input type="number" class="qty-input" data-item-id="${item.id}"
                 value="${quantity}" min="1" max="${item.stock_count}" step="1">
          <button class="qty-btn qty-plus" data-item-id="${item.id}" ${quantity >= item.stock_count ? 'disabled' : ''}>
            <span class="material-icons">add</span>
          </button>
        </div>
      `;

      // Click card to select/deselect (not on qty controls)
      card.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        if (e.target.closest('.qty-control')) return; // Don't toggle on qty click
        if (isOutOfStock) return;
        toggleItemSelection(item, card);
      });

      grid.appendChild(card);
    });

    // Attach qty control event listeners
    attachQtyListeners();
  }

  function toggleItemSelection(item, cardElement) {
    if (selectedItems[item.id]) {
      // Deselect
      delete selectedItems[item.id];
      cardElement.classList.remove('selected');
    } else {
      // Select
      const qtyInput = cardElement.querySelector('.qty-input');
      const quantity = parseInt(qtyInput.value) || 1;
      selectedItems[item.id] = {
        inventory_id: item.id,
        item_name: item.item_name,
        item_icon: item.item_icon,
        price: parseFloat(item.price),
        stock_count: item.stock_count,
        quantity: quantity
      };
      cardElement.classList.add('selected');
    }
    updateCheckoutBar();
  }

  function attachQtyListeners() {
    // Minus buttons
    document.querySelectorAll('.qty-minus').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        e.stopPropagation();
        const itemId = this.dataset.itemId;
        const input = document.querySelector(`.qty-input[data-item-id="${itemId}"]`);
        let val = parseInt(input.value) - 1;
        if (val < 1) val = 1;
        input.value = val;
        updateSelectedQuantity(itemId, val);
      });
    });

    // Plus buttons
    document.querySelectorAll('.qty-plus').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        e.stopPropagation();
        const itemId = this.dataset.itemId;
        const input = document.querySelector(`.qty-input[data-item-id="${itemId}"]`);
        const max = parseInt(input.max);
        let val = parseInt(input.value) + 1;
        if (val > max) val = max;
        input.value = val;
        updateSelectedQuantity(itemId, val);
      });
    });

    // Direct input change
    document.querySelectorAll('.qty-input').forEach(input => {
      input.addEventListener('change', function(e) {
        e.stopPropagation();
        const itemId = this.dataset.itemId;
        let val = parseInt(this.value);
        const max = parseInt(this.max);
        if (isNaN(val) || val < 1) val = 1;
        if (val > max) val = max;
        this.value = val;
        updateSelectedQuantity(itemId, val);
      });

      // Prevent card click when clicking input
      input.addEventListener('click', function(e) { e.stopPropagation(); });
    });
  }

  function updateSelectedQuantity(itemId, quantity) {
    if (selectedItems[itemId]) {
      selectedItems[itemId].quantity = quantity;
      updateCheckoutBar();
    }
  }

  function updateCheckoutBar() {
    const count = Object.keys(selectedItems).length;
    const bar = document.getElementById('checkoutBar');
    document.getElementById('selectedCount').textContent = count;
    bar.style.display = count > 0 ? 'flex' : 'none';
  }

  // Search
  let searchTimeout;
  document.getElementById('itemSearch').addEventListener('input', function() {
    clearTimeout(searchTimeout);
    searchTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
      currentPage = 1;
      loadItems(this.value.trim());
    }, 300);
  });

  // Pagination functions (render page buttons, handle clicks)
  function renderPagination(total, page, perPage) {
    const totalPages = Math.ceil(total / perPage);
    const container = document.getElementById('itemsPagination');
    container.innerHTML = '';

    if (totalPages <= 1) return;

    // Previous button
    const prevBtn = createPageBtn('Previous', page > 1, () => { currentPage--; loadItems(); });
    container.appendChild(prevBtn);

    // Page numbers (show max 5 around current)
    for (let i = Math.max(1, page-2); i <= Math.min(totalPages, page+2); i++) {
      const pageBtn = createPageBtn(i, true, () => { currentPage = i; loadItems(); });
      if (i === page) pageBtn.classList.add('active');
      container.appendChild(pageBtn);
    }

    // Next button
    const nextBtn = createPageBtn('Next', page < totalPages, () => { currentPage++; loadItems(); });
    container.appendChild(nextBtn);

    // Items count
    const info = document.createElement('span');
    info.className = 'pagination-info';
    info.textContent = `Showing ${(page-1)*perPage + 1}–${Math.min(page*perPage, total)} of ${total} items`;
    container.appendChild(info);
  }

  function createPageBtn(text, enabled, onClick) {
    const btn = document.createElement('button');
    btn.className = 'page-btn';
    btn.textContent = text;
    btn.disabled = !enabled;
    if (enabled) btn.addEventListener('click', onClick);
    return btn;
  }

  // Checkout button opens modal
  document.getElementById('checkoutBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
    if (Object.keys(selectedItems).length === 0) {
      showToast('Please select at least one item', 'warning');
      return;
    }
    renderCheckoutModal();
    openModal('checkoutModal');
  });

  function renderCheckoutModal() {
    const container = document.getElementById('checkoutItems');
    container.innerHTML = '';

    let totalQty = 0;
    let subtotal = 0;

    Object.values(selectedItems).forEach(item => {
      const itemSubtotal = item.price * item.quantity;
      totalQty += item.quantity;
      subtotal += itemSubtotal;

      const row = document.createElement('div');
      row.className = 'checkout-item-row';
      row.innerHTML = `
        <img src="${item.item_icon || '/assets/images/default-item.png'}" class="checkout-item-icon">
        <div class="checkout-item-details">
          <span class="checkout-item-name">${item.item_name}</span>
          <span class="checkout-item-qty">Qty: ${item.quantity} × ₱${item.price.toFixed(2)}</span>
        </div>
        <span class="checkout-item-subtotal">₱${itemSubtotal.toFixed(2)}</span>
        <button class="btn-icon btn-danger btn-sm checkout-item-remove" data-item-id="${item.inventory_id}">
          <span class="material-icons">close</span>
        </button>
      `;
      container.appendChild(row);
    });

    // Remove item from checkout
    container.querySelectorAll('.checkout-item-remove').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
        const itemId = this.dataset.itemId;
        delete selectedItems[itemId];
        // Also deselect the card visually
        const card = document.querySelector(`.item-card[data-item-id="${itemId}"]`);
        if (card) card.classList.remove('selected');
        updateCheckoutBar();
        if (Object.keys(selectedItems).length === 0) {
          closeModal('checkoutModal');
          return;
        }
        renderCheckoutModal(); // Re-render
      });
    });

    // Update summary
    document.getElementById('summaryItemCount').textContent = totalQty;
    document.getElementById('summarySubtotal').textContent = '₱' + subtotal.toFixed(2);
    updateTotalWithPayment();
  }

  // Payment type change affects delivery fee display
  document.querySelectorAll('input[name="paymentType"]').forEach(radio => {
    radio.addEventListener('change', function() {
      updateTotalWithPayment();
      // Show/hide address section based on payment type
      const addressSection = document.getElementById('addressSelect').closest('.checkout-section');
      const deliveryFeeRow = document.getElementById('deliveryFeeRow');
      if (this.value === 'pickup') {
        addressSection.style.display = 'none';
        deliveryFeeRow.style.display = 'none';
      } else {
        addressSection.style.display = 'block';
        deliveryFeeRow.style.display = 'flex';
      }
    });
  });

  function updateTotalWithPayment() {
    const paymentType = document.querySelector('input[name="paymentType"]:checked').value;
    const subtotalText = document.getElementById('summarySubtotal').textContent;
    const subtotal = parseFloat(subtotalText.replace('₱', '').replace(',', ''));
    const fee = paymentType === 'pickup' ? 0 : deliveryFee;
    document.getElementById('summaryDeliveryFee').textContent = '₱' + fee.toFixed(2);
    document.getElementById('summaryTotal').textContent = '₱' + (subtotal + fee).toFixed(2);
  }

  // Address dropdown: show custom input when "custom" selected
  document.getElementById('addressSelect').addEventListener('change', function() {
    const customWrap = document.getElementById('customAddressWrap');
    customWrap.style.display = this.value === 'custom' ? 'block' : 'none';
  });

  // Place Order button
  document.getElementById('placeOrderBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
    const items = Object.values(selectedItems).map(item => ({
      inventory_id: item.inventory_id,
      quantity: item.quantity
    }));

    const paymentType = document.querySelector('input[name="paymentType"]:checked').value;

    // Determine delivery address
    let deliveryAddress = null;
    if (paymentType !== 'pickup') {
      const addressSelect = document.getElementById('addressSelect');
      if (addressSelect.value === 'custom') {
        deliveryAddress = document.getElementById('customAddress').value.trim();
        if (!deliveryAddress) {
          showToast('Please enter a delivery address', 'warning');
          return;
        }
      } else {
        // Send the address_id — server will look up the full address
        deliveryAddress = addressSelect.value; // This is the address_id
      }
    }

    const orderNotes = document.getElementById('orderNotes').value.trim();

    // Disable button, show loading
    this.disabled = true;
    this.innerHTML = '<div class="spinner" style="width:20px;height:20px;"></div> Placing Order...';

    // First: real-time stock validation
    const itemIds = items.map(i => i.inventory_id).join(',');
    ajaxGet('/api/inventory/check_stock.php', { item_ids: itemIds })
      .then(stockData => {
        // Check for out-of-stock items
        const unavailable = [];
        stockData.items.forEach(stockItem => {
          const selected = selectedItems[stockItem.id];
          if (!selected) return;
          if (stockItem.status !== 'active' || stockItem.stock < selected.quantity) {
            unavailable.push(selected.item_name);
            delete selectedItems[stockItem.id];
          }
        });

        if (unavailable.length > 0) {
          Swal.fire({
            icon: 'warning',
            title: 'Items Unavailable',
            html: `The following items are no longer available and have been removed from your order:<br><br><strong>${unavailable.join('<br>')}</strong>`,
            confirmButtonColor: 'var(--primary)'
          });
          renderCheckoutModal();
          updateCheckoutBar();
          resetPlaceOrderBtn();
          if (Object.keys(selectedItems).length === 0) {
            closeModal('checkoutModal');
          }
          return;
        }

        // All items valid — place the order
        return ajaxPost('/api/orders/place_order.php', {
          items: JSON.stringify(items),
          payment_type: paymentType,
          delivery_address: deliveryAddress,
          order_notes: orderNotes
        });
      })
      .then(data => {
        if (!data) return; // Stock validation failed, already handled
        if (data.success) {
          closeModal('checkoutModal');
          Swal.fire({
            icon: 'success',
            title: 'Order Placed Successfully!',
            html: `Your order <strong>#${data.order_id}</strong> has been sent to staff for confirmation.`,
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonText: 'View Receipt',
            cancelButtonText: 'Go to My Orders',
            confirmButtonColor: 'var(--primary)'
          }).then(result => {
            if (result.isConfirmed) {
              window.open('/receipt.php?token=' + data.receipt_token, '_blank');
              window.location.href = 'my_orders.php';
            } else {
              window.location.href = 'my_orders.php';
            }
          });
        } else {
          showToast(data.message || 'Failed to place order', 'error');
          resetPlaceOrderBtn();
        }
      })
      .catch(err => {
        showToast('An error occurred. Please try again.', 'error');
        resetPlaceOrderBtn();
      });
  });

  function resetPlaceOrderBtn() {
    const btn = document.getElementById('placeOrderBtn');
    btn.disabled = false;
    btn.innerHTML = '<span class="material-icons">check</span> Place Order';
  }

  function preselectReorderItems(reorderItems) {
    reorderItems.forEach(item => {
      const card = document.querySelector(`.item-card[data-item-id="${item.inventory_id}"]`);
      if (card && !card.classList.contains('out-of-stock')) {
        const qtyInput = card.querySelector('.qty-input');
        qtyInput.value = Math.min(item.quantity, parseInt(qtyInput.max));
        selectedItems[item.inventory_id] = {
          inventory_id: item.inventory_id,
          item_name: item.item_name,
          item_icon: item.item_icon,
          price: item.price,
          stock_count: parseInt(qtyInput.max),
          quantity: parseInt(qtyInput.value)
        };
        card.classList.add('selected');
      }
    });
    updateCheckoutBar();
  }

  function showLoading() {
    document.getElementById('itemsLoading').style.display = 'flex';
  }
  function hideLoading() {
    document.getElementById('itemsLoading').style.display = 'none';
  }

});
```

---

### 3. `customer/my_orders.php`

**PHP Logic (top of file):**
```
1. Include auth_check, require_role([ROLE_CUSTOMER])
2. Account status check — pending accounts can see this but it will be empty.
   Flagged accounts can view orders but cannot cancel anymore (well, they can cancel pending ones but
   each cancel risks further flagging — the API handles the logic, the UI just shows the buttons).
3. Include header, sidebar
```

**HTML Structure:**
```html
<div class="main-content">
  <div class="page-header">
    <h1>My Orders</h1>
    <p class="text-muted">Track and manage your current orders.</p>
  </div>

  <!-- Filter Bar -->
  <div class="filter-bar" id="orderFilters">
    <button class="filter-btn active" data-filter="all">All</button>
    <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="pending">Pending</button>
    <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="confirmed">Confirmed</button>
    <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="assigned">Assigned</button>
    <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="on_delivery">On Delivery</button>
    <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="ready_for_pickup">Ready for Pickup</button>
  </div>

  <!-- Bulk Actions Bar (shown when checkboxes selected) -->
  <div class="bulk-actions-bar" id="bulkActions" style="display: none;">
    <span id="bulkSelectedCount">0</span> order(s) selected
    <button class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" id="bulkCancelBtn">Cancel Selected</button>
  </div>

  <!-- Orders Table -->
  <div class="data-table-wrapper">
    <table class="data-table" id="ordersTable">
      <thead>
        <tr>
          <th><input type="checkbox" class="custom-checkbox" id="selectAllOrders"></th>
          <th>Order ID</th>
          <th>Items</th>
          <th>Payment</th>
          <th>Status</th>
          <th>Quantity</th>
          <th>Rider</th>
          <th>Order Date</th>
          <th>Expected Delivery</th>
          <th>Staff Note</th>
          <th>Actions</th>
        </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody id="ordersBody">
        <!-- Loaded by JS via AJAX -->
        <tr class="loading-row">
          <td colspan="11"><div class="spinner"></div></td>
        </tr>
      </tbody>
    </table>
  </div>

  <!-- Pagination -->
  <div class="pagination" id="ordersPagination"></div>

  <!-- Empty State (shown when no orders) -->
  <div class="empty-state" id="emptyOrders" style="display: none;">
    <span class="material-icons">inbox</span>
    <p>No orders found.</p>
    <a href="place_order.php" class="btn btn-primary">Place an Order</a>
  </div>
</div>
```

### `customer/css/my_orders.css`

```
.filter-bar:
  - Horizontal scrollable on mobile (overflow-x auto)
  - Gap between filter buttons
  - .filter-btn: pill shape, border, cursor pointer
  - .filter-btn.active: matches the status color of the filter
    (e.g., Pending filter active = orange background)

.bulk-actions-bar:
  - Glass card, flex row, align center, gap
  - Padding 12px 20px
  - Margin bottom 16px
  - Slide-down animation when shown

.data-table:
  - Full width, border-collapse
  - th: background slightly darker surface, sticky top
  - td: padding 12px 16px
  - Alternating row colors
  - Hover row highlight
  - .item-with-icon within td: flex inline, align center

Actions column:
  - .btn-icon: 32x32px buttons with centered Material icon
  - Green check icon (accept/received)
  - Red X icon (cancel)
  - Gap between action buttons

Responsive:
  - Table wrapper has horizontal scroll
  - Actions column minimum width to prevent button wrapping
```

### `customer/js/my_orders.js`

```javascript
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {

  let currentFilter = 'all';
  let currentPage = 1;
  const perPage = 50; // ITEMS_PER_PAGE

  // Load orders on page load
  loadOrders();

  // Filter buttons
  document.querySelectorAll('#orderFilters .filter-btn').forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      document.querySelectorAll('#orderFilters .filter-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
      this.classList.add('active');
      currentFilter = this.dataset.filter;
      currentPage = 1;
      loadOrders();
    });
  });

  function loadOrders() {
    const params = {
      status: currentFilter === 'all' ? '' : currentFilter,
      page: currentPage
    };

    // Show loading
    document.getElementById('ordersBody').innerHTML =
      '<tr class="loading-row"><td colspan="11"><div class="spinner"></div></td></tr>';
    document.getElementById('emptyOrders').style.display = 'none';

    ajaxGet('/api/orders/get_orders.php', params)
      .then(data => {
        if (data.orders.length === 0) {
          document.getElementById('ordersBody').innerHTML = '';
          document.getElementById('emptyOrders').style.display = 'flex';
          document.getElementById('ordersPagination').innerHTML = '';
          return;
        }

        document.getElementById('emptyOrders').style.display = 'none';
        renderOrders(data.orders);
        renderOrdersPagination(data.total, data.page, data.per_page);
      })
      .catch(err => {
        showToast('Failed to load orders', 'error');
      });
  }

  function renderOrders(orders) {
    const tbody = document.getElementById('ordersBody');
    tbody.innerHTML = '';

    orders.forEach(order => {
      const tr = document.createElement('tr');

      // Determine which actions are available
      const canCancel = (order.status === 'pending'); // Customer can only cancel pending
      const canAccept = (order.status === 'delivered' || order.status === 'picked_up')
                        && !order.customer_confirmed;

      // Items display: combine all order_items into one cell
      const itemsHtml = order.items.map(item => `
        <span class="item-with-icon">
          <img src="${item.item_icon || '/assets/images/default-item.png'}" class="item-icon-sm">
          ${item.item_name}
        </span>
      `).join(', ');

      // Total quantity across all items in this order
      const totalQty = order.items.reduce((sum, item) => sum + parseInt(item.quantity), 0);

      // Payment label
      const paymentLabels = { cod: 'Cash on Delivery', pickup: 'Pickup at Store', online: 'Online' };

      tr.innerHTML = `
        <td>
          ${canCancel ? `<input type="checkbox" class="custom-checkbox order-checkbox" data-order-id="${order.id}">` : ''}
        </td>
        <td><strong>#${order.id}</strong></td>
        <td>${itemsHtml}</td>
        <td>${paymentLabels[order.payment_type] || order.payment_type}</td>
        <td><span class="badge badge-${order.status.replace(/_/g, '-')}">${formatStatus(order.status)}</span></td>
        <td>${totalQty}</td>
        <td>${order.rider_name || '<span class="text-muted">Unassigned</span>'}</td>
        <td>${formatDate(order.order_date)}</td>
        <td>${order.expected_delivery_date ? formatDate(order.expected_delivery_date) : '<span class="text-muted">—</span>'}</td>
        <td>${order.staff_comment || '<span class="text-muted">—</span>'}</td>
        <td class="actions-cell">
          ${canAccept ? `
            <button class="btn-icon btn-success" title="Mark as Received" onclick="acceptOrder(${order.id})">
              <span class="material-icons">check_circle</span>
            </button>
          ` : ''}
          ${canCancel ? `
            <button class="btn-icon btn-danger" title="Cancel Order" onclick="cancelOrder(${order.id})">
              <span class="material-icons">cancel</span>
            </button>
          ` : ''}
          ${order.status === 'cancelled' || order.status === 'delivered' || order.status === 'accepted' || order.status === 'picked_up' ? `
            <button class="btn-icon btn-info" title="Reorder" onclick="reorder(${order.id})">
              <span class="material-icons">replay</span>
            </button>
          ` : ''}
          <button class="btn-icon btn-outline" title="View Receipt" onclick="viewReceipt('${order.receipt_token}')">
            <span class="material-icons">receipt</span>
          </button>
        </td>
      `;

      tbody.appendChild(tr);
    });

    // Init bulk select
    initBulkSelect('ordersTable');
  }

  // Cancel Order
  window.cancelOrder = function(orderId) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Cancel Order #' + orderId + '?',
      html: `
        <p style="margin-bottom: 12px; color: var(--text-secondary);">
          This action cannot be undone. Please provide a reason for cancellation.
        </p>
        <textarea id="cancelReason" class="swal2-textarea"
          placeholder="Reason for cancellation (required)" rows="3"></textarea>
      `,
      icon: 'warning',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Yes, Cancel Order',
      cancelButtonText: 'No, Keep It',
      confirmButtonColor: '#EF5350',
      preConfirm: () => {
        const reason = document.getElementById('cancelReason').value.trim();
        if (!reason) {
          Swal.showValidationMessage('Please provide a cancellation reason');
          return false;
        }
        return reason;
      }
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/orders/cancel_order.php', {
          order_id: orderId,
          reason: result.value
        }).then(data => {
          if (data.success) {
            showToast('Order cancelled successfully', 'success');
            loadOrders(); // Refresh table
            // Check if account was flagged
            if (data.account_flagged) {
              Swal.fire({
                icon: 'warning',
                title: 'Account Flagged',
                text: 'You have reached the maximum number of cancellations. Your ordering privileges have been suspended. You can submit an appeal from the Dashboard.',
                confirmButtonColor: 'var(--warning)'
              });
            }
          } else {
            showToast(data.message || 'Failed to cancel order', 'error');
          }
        });
      }
    });
  };

  // Accept/Received
  window.acceptOrder = function(orderId) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Confirm Receipt',
      text: 'Mark this order as received/accepted? This is optional and just confirms you got your items.',
      icon: 'question',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Yes, I Received It',
      cancelButtonText: 'Not Yet',
      confirmButtonColor: 'var(--success)'
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/orders/confirm_received.php', { order_id: orderId })
          .then(data => {
            if (data.success) {
              showToast('Order marked as received!', 'success');
              loadOrders();
            } else {
              showToast(data.message || 'Failed to confirm receipt', 'error');
            }
          });
      }
    });
  };

  // Reorder
  window.reorder = function(orderId) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Reorder',
      text: 'Would you like to place a new order with the same items?',
      icon: 'question',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Yes, Reorder',
      confirmButtonColor: 'var(--primary)'
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        window.location.href = 'place_order.php?reorder=' + orderId;
      }
    });
  };

  // View Receipt
  window.viewReceipt = function(token) {
    window.open('/receipt.php?token=' + token, '_blank');
  };

  // Bulk cancel
  document.getElementById('bulkCancelBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
    const selectedIds = getSelectedIds('ordersTable');
    if (selectedIds.length === 0) {
      showToast('No orders selected', 'warning');
      return;
    }

    Swal.fire({
      title: `Cancel ${selectedIds.length} Order(s)?`,
      html: `<textarea id="bulkCancelReason" class="swal2-textarea"
              placeholder="Reason for cancellation (required)" rows="3"></textarea>`,
      icon: 'warning',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Cancel All Selected',
      confirmButtonColor: '#EF5350',
      preConfirm: () => {
        const reason = document.getElementById('bulkCancelReason').value.trim();
        if (!reason) {
          Swal.showValidationMessage('Please provide a reason');
          return false;
        }
        return reason;
      }
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/orders/bulk_update.php', {
          order_ids: JSON.stringify(selectedIds),
          action: 'cancel',
          reason: result.value
        }).then(data => {
          if (data.success !== undefined) {
            showToast(`${data.success} order(s) cancelled`, 'success');
            loadOrders();
          }
        });
      }
    });
  });

  // Select all checkbox handler
  document.getElementById('selectAllOrders').addEventListener('change', function() {
    const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.order-checkbox');
    checkboxes.forEach(cb => { cb.checked = this.checked; });
    updateBulkBar();
  });

  // Delegate individual checkbox changes
  document.getElementById('ordersBody').addEventListener('change', function(e) {
    if (e.target.classList.contains('order-checkbox')) {
      updateBulkBar();
    }
  });

  function updateBulkBar() {
    const checked = document.querySelectorAll('.order-checkbox:checked').length;
    const bar = document.getElementById('bulkActions');
    bar.style.display = checked > 0 ? 'flex' : 'none';
    document.getElementById('bulkSelectedCount').textContent = checked;
  }

  // Helper functions
  function formatStatus(status) {
    const labels = {
      pending: 'Pending',
      confirmed: 'Confirmed',
      assigned: 'Assigned',
      on_delivery: 'On Delivery',
      delivered: 'Delivered',
      accepted: 'Accepted',
      ready_for_pickup: 'Ready for Pickup',
      picked_up: 'Picked Up',
      cancelled: 'Cancelled'
    };
    return labels[status] || status;
  }

  function formatDate(dateStr) {
    if (!dateStr) return '—';
    const d = new Date(dateStr);
    return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 'numeric', year: 'numeric' })
      + ' ' + d.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
  }

  function renderOrdersPagination(total, page, perPage) {
    // Same pagination rendering logic as place_order.js
    const totalPages = Math.ceil(total / perPage);
    const container = document.getElementById('ordersPagination');
    container.innerHTML = '';
    if (totalPages <= 1) return;

    const prevBtn = document.createElement('button');
    prevBtn.className = 'page-btn';
    prevBtn.textContent = 'Previous';
    prevBtn.disabled = page <= 1;
    prevBtn.addEventListener('click', () => { currentPage--; loadOrders(); });
    container.appendChild(prevBtn);

    for (let i = Math.max(1, page-2); i <= Math.min(totalPages, page+2); i++) {
      const pb = document.createElement('button');
      pb.className = `page-btn ${i === page ? 'active' : ''}`;
      pb.textContent = i;
      pb.addEventListener('click', () => { currentPage = i; loadOrders(); });
      container.appendChild(pb);
    }

    const nextBtn = document.createElement('button');
    nextBtn.className = 'page-btn';
    nextBtn.textContent = 'Next';
    nextBtn.disabled = page >= totalPages;
    nextBtn.addEventListener('click', () => { currentPage++; loadOrders(); });
    container.appendChild(nextBtn);

    const info = document.createElement('span');
    info.className = 'pagination-info';
    info.textContent = `Showing ${(page-1)*perPage + 1}–${Math.min(page*perPage, total)} of ${total} orders`;
    container.appendChild(info);
  }

});
```

---

### 4. `customer/order_history.php`

**PHP Logic:**
```
1. Include auth_check, require_role([ROLE_CUSTOMER])
2. Include header, sidebar
```

**HTML Structure:**
```html
<div class="main-content">
  <div class="page-header">
    <h1>Order History</h1>
    <p class="text-muted">View all your past orders and their details.</p>
  </div>

  <!-- Toolbar: Filters + Search + Date Range -->
  <div class="toolbar">
    <div class="filter-bar" id="historyFilters">
      <button class="filter-btn active" data-filter="all">All</button>
      <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="delivered">Delivered</button>
      <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="accepted">Accepted</button>
      <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="picked_up">Picked Up</button>
      <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="cancelled">Cancelled</button>
    </div>
    <div class="toolbar-right">
      <div class="search-bar">
        <span class="material-icons search-icon">search</span>
        <input type="text" id="historySearch" class="search-input" placeholder="Search by Order ID or item...">
      </div>
      <div class="date-range">
        <input type="date" id="dateFrom" class="float-input" title="From Date">
        <span class="text-muted">to</span>
        <input type="date" id="dateTo" class="float-input" title="To Date">
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

  <!-- History Table -->
  <div class="data-table-wrapper">
    <table class="data-table" id="historyTable">
      <thead>
        <tr>
          <th>Order ID</th>
          <th>Items</th>
          <th>Payment</th>
          <th>Delivery Type</th>
          <th>Status</th>
          <th>Total Qty</th>
          <th>Total Amount</th>
          <th>Rider</th>
          <th>Order Date</th>
          <th>Delivered Date</th>
          <th>Cancellation Reason</th>
          <th>Cancelled By</th>
          <th>Actions</th>
        </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody id="historyBody">
        <tr class="loading-row"><td colspan="13"><div class="spinner"></div></td></tr>
      </tbody>
    </table>
  </div>

  <div class="pagination" id="historyPagination"></div>

  <div class="empty-state" id="emptyHistory" style="display: none;">
    <span class="material-icons">history</span>
    <p>No order history found.</p>
  </div>
</div>
```

### `customer/css/order_history.css`

```
.toolbar:
  - Flex column on mobile, row on desktop
  - Gap between filter bar and right side
  - .toolbar-right: flex row, gap, align center

.date-range:
  - Flex row, gap 8px, align center
  - Input type date styled to match theme

Table specific:
  - Cancellation reason column: max-width 200px, text truncated with ellipsis, hover tooltip shows full text
  - Cancelled By column: show role badge + name
  - Total Amount column: font-weight bold, primary color

Responsive: same table horizontal scroll pattern
```

### `customer/js/order_history.js`

```javascript
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {

  let currentFilter = 'all';
  let currentPage = 1;
  let searchText = '';
  let dateFrom = '';
  let dateTo = '';

  loadHistory();

  // Filter buttons
  document.querySelectorAll('#historyFilters .filter-btn').forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      document.querySelectorAll('#historyFilters .filter-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
      this.classList.add('active');
      currentFilter = this.dataset.filter;
      currentPage = 1;
      loadHistory();
    });
  });

  // Search (debounced)
  let searchTimeout;
  document.getElementById('historySearch').addEventListener('input', function() {
    clearTimeout(searchTimeout);
    searchTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
      searchText = this.value.trim();
      currentPage = 1;
      loadHistory();
    }, 300);
  });

  // Date range
  document.getElementById('dateFrom').addEventListener('change', function() {
    dateFrom = this.value;
    currentPage = 1;
    loadHistory();
  });
  document.getElementById('dateTo').addEventListener('change', function() {
    dateTo = this.value;
    currentPage = 1;
    loadHistory();
  });

  function loadHistory() {
    const params = {
      status: currentFilter === 'all' ? '' : currentFilter,
      search: searchText,
      page: currentPage,
      date_from: dateFrom,
      date_to: dateTo,
      scope: 'history' // Tell the API to include completed/cancelled orders
    };

    document.getElementById('historyBody').innerHTML =
      '<tr class="loading-row"><td colspan="13"><div class="spinner"></div></td></tr>';
    document.getElementById('emptyHistory').style.display = 'none';

    ajaxGet('/api/orders/get_orders.php', params)
      .then(data => {
        if (data.orders.length === 0) {
          document.getElementById('historyBody').innerHTML = '';
          document.getElementById('emptyHistory').style.display = 'flex';
          document.getElementById('historyPagination').innerHTML = '';
          return;
        }

        document.getElementById('emptyHistory').style.display = 'none';
        renderHistory(data.orders);
        renderPagination(data.total, data.page, data.per_page, 'historyPagination', loadHistory);
      })
      .catch(() => showToast('Failed to load order history', 'error'));
  }

  function renderHistory(orders) {
    const tbody = document.getElementById('historyBody');
    tbody.innerHTML = '';

    orders.forEach(order => {
      const itemsHtml = order.items.map(item =>
        `<span class="item-with-icon"><img src="${item.item_icon || '/assets/images/default-item.png'}" class="item-icon-sm">${item.item_name}</span>`
      ).join(', ');

      const totalQty = order.items.reduce((sum, i) => sum + parseInt(i.quantity), 0);
      const paymentLabels = { cod: 'Cash on Delivery', pickup: 'Pickup at Store', online: 'Online' };
      const deliveryLabels = { delivery: 'Delivery', pickup: 'Pickup' };

      const tr = document.createElement('tr');
      tr.innerHTML = `
        <td><strong>#${order.id}</strong></td>
        <td>${itemsHtml}</td>
        <td>${paymentLabels[order.payment_type] || order.payment_type}</td>
        <td>${deliveryLabels[order.delivery_type] || order.delivery_type}</td>
        <td><span class="badge badge-${order.status.replace(/_/g, '-')}">${formatStatus(order.status)}</span></td>
        <td>${totalQty}</td>
        <td><strong>${formatCurrency(order.total_amount)}</strong></td>
        <td>${order.rider_name || '<span class="text-muted">N/A</span>'}</td>
        <td>${formatDate(order.order_date)}</td>
        <td>${order.delivered_at ? formatDate(order.delivered_at) : '<span class="text-muted">—</span>'}</td>
        <td class="truncate-cell" title="${order.cancellation_reason || ''}">${order.cancellation_reason || '<span class="text-muted">—</span>'}</td>
        <td>${order.cancelled_by_name ? order.cancelled_by_name : '<span class="text-muted">—</span>'}</td>
        <td class="actions-cell">
          <button class="btn-icon btn-info" title="Reorder" onclick="reorder(${order.id})">
            <span class="material-icons">replay</span>
          </button>
          <button class="btn-icon btn-outline" title="View Receipt" onclick="viewReceipt('${order.receipt_token}')">
            <span class="material-icons">receipt</span>
          </button>
        </td>
      `;
      tbody.appendChild(tr);
    });
  }

  // Reorder and receipt functions (same as my_orders.js)
  window.reorder = function(orderId) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Reorder',
      text: 'Place a new order with the same items?',
      icon: 'question',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Yes, Reorder',
      confirmButtonColor: 'var(--primary)'
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        window.location.href = 'place_order.php?reorder=' + orderId;
      }
    });
  };

  window.viewReceipt = function(token) {
    window.open('/receipt.php?token=' + token, '_blank');
  };

  // Shared helpers
  function formatStatus(s) {
    const labels = { pending:'Pending', confirmed:'Confirmed', assigned:'Assigned', on_delivery:'On Delivery', delivered:'Delivered', accepted:'Accepted', ready_for_pickup:'Ready for Pickup', picked_up:'Picked Up', cancelled:'Cancelled' };
    return labels[s] || s;
  }
  function formatDate(d) {
    if (!d) return '—';
    return new Date(d).toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month:'short', day:'numeric', year:'numeric' }) + ' ' + new Date(d).toLocaleTimeString('en-US', { hour:'2-digit', minute:'2-digit' });
  }
  function formatCurrency(a) { return '₱' + parseFloat(a).toFixed(2); }

  function renderPagination(total, page, perPage, containerId, loadFunc) {
    const totalPages = Math.ceil(total / perPage);
    const container = document.getElementById(containerId);
    container.innerHTML = '';
    if (totalPages <= 1) return;

    const prev = document.createElement('button');
    prev.className = 'page-btn'; prev.textContent = 'Previous'; prev.disabled = page <= 1;
    prev.addEventListener('click', () => { currentPage--; loadFunc(); });
    container.appendChild(prev);

    for (let i = Math.max(1,page-2); i <= Math.min(totalPages,page+2); i++) {
      const pb = document.createElement('button');
      pb.className = `page-btn ${i===page?'active':''}`;
      pb.textContent = i;
      pb.addEventListener('click', () => { currentPage = i; loadFunc(); });
      container.appendChild(pb);
    }

    const next = document.createElement('button');
    next.className = 'page-btn'; next.textContent = 'Next'; next.disabled = page >= totalPages;
    next.addEventListener('click', () => { currentPage++; loadFunc(); });
    container.appendChild(next);

    const info = document.createElement('span');
    info.className = 'pagination-info';
    info.textContent = `Showing ${(page-1)*perPage+1}–${Math.min(page*perPage,total)} of ${total}`;
    container.appendChild(info);
  }

});
```

---

### 5. `customer/settings.php`

**PHP Logic (top of file):**
```
1. Include auth_check, require_role([ROLE_CUSTOMER])
2. Fetch current user data from DB (fresh, not just session — in case it was updated elsewhere)
3. Fetch customer addresses from DB
4. Fetch user preferences from DB
5. If status is flagged: fetch appeal history
6. Include header, sidebar
```

**HTML Structure:**
```html
<div class="main-content">
  <div class="page-header">
    <h1>Settings</h1>
    <p class="text-muted">Manage your profile, addresses, and preferences.</p>
  </div>

  <!-- Profile Section -->
  <div class="settings-section glass-card">
    <h2><span class="material-icons">person</span> Profile Information</h2>
    <form id="profileForm">
      <div class="form-grid">
        <div class="float-input-group">
          <input type="text" id="profileUsername" class="float-input" value="{username}" disabled
                 style="opacity: 0.6; cursor: not-allowed;">
          <label class="float-label">Username (cannot be changed)</label>
        </div>
        <div class="float-input-group">
          <input type="text" id="profileFullName" class="float-input" value="{full_name}" placeholder=" " required>
          <label class="float-label">Full Name</label>
        </div>
        <div class="float-input-group">
          <input type="email" id="profileEmail" class="float-input" value="{email}" placeholder=" " required>
          <label class="float-label">Email</label>
        </div>
        <div class="float-input-group">
          <input type="tel" id="profilePhone" class="float-input" value="{phone}" placeholder=" " required>
          <label class="float-label">Phone Number</label>
        </div>
      </div>
      <button type="submit" class="btn btn-primary">
        <span class="material-icons">save</span> Save Changes
      </button>
    </form>
  </div>

  <!-- Password Section -->
  <div class="settings-section glass-card">
    <h2><span class="material-icons">lock</span> Change Password</h2>
    <form id="passwordForm">
      <div class="form-grid">
        <div class="float-input-group">
          <input type="password" id="currentPassword" class="float-input" placeholder=" " required>
          <label class="float-label">Current Password</label>
        </div>
        <div class="float-input-group">
          <input type="password" id="newPassword" class="float-input" placeholder=" " required>
          <label class="float-label">New Password (min. 6 characters)</label>
        </div>
        <div class="float-input-group">
          <input type="password" id="confirmPassword" class="float-input" placeholder=" " required>
          <label class="float-label">Confirm New Password</label>
        </div>
      </div>
      <button type="submit" class="btn btn-warning">
        <span class="material-icons">lock_reset</span> Change Password
      </button>
    </form>
  </div>

  <!-- Addresses Section -->
  <div class="settings-section glass-card">
    <h2><span class="material-icons">location_on</span> Delivery Addresses</h2>

    <div class="addresses-list" id="addressesList">
      <!-- Rendered by PHP or JS -->
      <!-- For each address: -->
      <div class="address-card" data-address-id="{id}">
        <div class="address-info">
          <span class="address-label">{label}</span>
          {if is_default: <span class="badge badge-confirmed">Default</span>}
          <p class="address-text">{full_address}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="address-actions">
          {if not default: <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline set-default-btn" data-id="{id}">Set Default</button>}
          <button class="btn btn-sm btn-info edit-address-btn" data-id="{id}">
            <span class="material-icons">edit</span>
          </button>
          <button class="btn btn-sm btn-danger delete-address-btn" data-id="{id}">
            <span class="material-icons">delete</span>
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
      <!-- End foreach -->
    </div>

    <button class="btn btn-outline" id="addAddressBtn">
      <span class="material-icons">add</span> Add Address
    </button>
  </div>

  <!-- Appeal Section (only if flagged) -->
  <?php if ($user['status'] === 'flagged'): ?>
  <div class="settings-section glass-card flagged-section">
    <h2><span class="material-icons">gavel</span> Cancellation Appeals</h2>
    <p>Your account is flagged due to excessive cancellations (<strong><?= $user['cancellation_count'] ?></strong> this month, max: <strong><?= get_setting('max_cancellation') ?></strong>).</p>

    <div class="appeals-history" id="appealsHistory">
      <!-- Table of past appeals -->
      <table class="data-table">
        <thead>
          <tr>
            <th>Date</th>
            <th>Reason</th>
            <th>Status</th>
            <th>Admin Notes</th>
          </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>
          <!-- PHP foreach appeals: -->
          <tr>
            <td>{formatted created_at}</td>
            <td>{reason}</td>
            <td><span class="badge badge-{status}">{status}</span></td>
            <td>{admin_notes or '—'}</td>
          </tr>
        </tbody>
      </table>
    </div>

    <!-- Show submit button only if no pending appeal -->
    <?php if (!$has_pending_appeal): ?>
    <button class="btn btn-warning" id="settingsAppealBtn">
      <span class="material-icons">send</span> Submit New Appeal
    </button>
    <?php else: ?>
    <p class="text-muted"><span class="material-icons" style="vertical-align:middle;">hourglass_top</span> You have a pending appeal awaiting review.</p>
    <?php endif; ?>
  </div>
  <?php endif; ?>
</div>
```

### `customer/js/settings.js`

```javascript
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {

  // ===== PROFILE FORM =====
  document.getElementById('profileForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    const data = {
      full_name: document.getElementById('profileFullName').value.trim(),
      email: document.getElementById('profileEmail').value.trim(),
      phone: document.getElementById('profilePhone').value.trim()
    };

    if (!data.full_name || !data.email || !data.phone) {
      showToast('All fields are required', 'warning');
      return;
    }

    ajaxPost('/api/settings/update_profile.php', data)
      .then(res => {
        if (res.success) {
          showToast('Profile updated successfully', 'success');
        } else {
          showToast(res.message || 'Failed to update profile', 'error');
        }
      });
  });

  // ===== PASSWORD FORM =====
  document.getElementById('passwordForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    const current = document.getElementById('currentPassword').value;
    const newPass = document.getElementById('newPassword').value;
    const confirm = document.getElementById('confirmPassword').value;

    if (!current || !newPass || !confirm) {
      showToast('All password fields are required', 'warning');
      return;
    }
    if (newPass.length < 6) {
      showToast('New password must be at least 6 characters', 'warning');
      return;
    }
    if (newPass !== confirm) {
      showToast('New passwords do not match', 'warning');
      return;
    }

    ajaxPost('/api/settings/change_password.php', {
      current_password: current,
      new_password: newPass,
      confirm_password: confirm
    }).then(res => {
      if (res.success) {
        showToast('Password changed successfully', 'success');
        document.getElementById('passwordForm').reset();
      } else {
        showToast(res.message || 'Failed to change password', 'error');
      }
    });
  });

  // ===== ADDRESSES =====

  // Add Address
  document.getElementById('addAddressBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Add New Address',
      html: `
        <div class="float-input-group" style="margin-bottom:12px;">
          <input type="text" id="newAddrLabel" class="swal2-input" placeholder="Label (e.g., Home, Office)">
        </div>
        <div class="float-input-group">
          <textarea id="newAddrFull" class="swal2-textarea" placeholder="Full address" rows="3"></textarea>
        </div>
        <label style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;margin-top:12px;">
          <input type="checkbox" id="newAddrDefault"> Set as default address
        </label>
      `,
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Add Address',
      confirmButtonColor: 'var(--primary)',
      preConfirm: () => {
        const label = document.getElementById('newAddrLabel').value.trim();
        const address = document.getElementById('newAddrFull').value.trim();
        if (!label || !address) {
          Swal.showValidationMessage('Label and address are required');
          return false;
        }
        return {
          label: label,
          full_address: address,
          is_default: document.getElementById('newAddrDefault').checked ? 1 : 0
        };
      }
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/addresses/add.php', result.value)
          .then(res => {
            if (res.success) {
              showToast('Address added', 'success');
              location.reload();
            } else {
              showToast(res.message || 'Failed to add address', 'error');
            }
          });
      }
    });
  });

  // Edit Address (delegated)
  document.querySelectorAll('.edit-address-btn').forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      const card = this.closest('.address-card');
      const id = this.dataset.id;
      const label = card.querySelector('.address-label').textContent;
      const address = card.querySelector('.address-text').textContent;

      Swal.fire({
        title: 'Edit Address',
        html: `
          <input type="text" id="editAddrLabel" class="swal2-input" value="${label}" placeholder="Label">
          <textarea id="editAddrFull" class="swal2-textarea" rows="3" placeholder="Full address">${address}</textarea>
        `,
        showCancelButton: true,
        confirmButtonText: 'Save',
        confirmButtonColor: 'var(--primary)',
        preConfirm: () => {
          const newLabel = document.getElementById('editAddrLabel').value.trim();
          const newAddr = document.getElementById('editAddrFull').value.trim();
          if (!newLabel || !newAddr) {
            Swal.showValidationMessage('Both fields are required');
            return false;
          }
          return { address_id: id, label: newLabel, full_address: newAddr };
        }
      }).then(result => {
        if (result.isConfirmed) {
          ajaxPost('/api/addresses/update.php', result.value)
            .then(res => {
              if (res.success) {
                showToast('Address updated', 'success');
                location.reload();
              } else {
                showToast(res.message || 'Failed to update', 'error');
              }
            });
        }
      });
    });
  });

  // Delete Address (delegated)
  document.querySelectorAll('.delete-address-btn').forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      const id = this.dataset.id;
      Swal.fire({
        title: 'Delete Address?',
        text: 'This address will be permanently removed.',
        icon: 'warning',
        showCancelButton: true,
        confirmButtonText: 'Delete',
        confirmButtonColor: '#EF5350'
      }).then(result => {
        if (result.isConfirmed) {
          ajaxPost('/api/addresses/delete.php', { address_id: id })
            .then(res => {
              if (res.success) {
                showToast('Address deleted', 'success');
                location.reload();
              } else {
                showToast(res.message || 'Cannot delete address', 'error');
              }
            });
        }
      });
    });
  });

  // Set Default (delegated)
  document.querySelectorAll('.set-default-btn').forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      const id = this.dataset.id;
      ajaxPost('/api/addresses/update.php', { address_id: id, is_default: 1 })
        .then(res => {
          if (res.success) {
            showToast('Default address updated', 'success');
            location.reload();
          } else {
            showToast(res.message || 'Failed', 'error');
          }
        });
    });
  });

  // ===== APPEAL (if flagged) =====
  const appealBtn = document.getElementById('settingsAppealBtn');
  if (appealBtn) {
    appealBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      Swal.fire({
        title: 'Submit Cancellation Appeal',
        html: `
          <p style="margin-bottom:12px;color:var(--text-secondary);">
            Explain why your cancellations were necessary.
          </p>
          <textarea id="appealReason" class="swal2-textarea" placeholder="Your reason..." rows="5"></textarea>
        `,
        showCancelButton: true,
        confirmButtonText: 'Submit Appeal',
        confirmButtonColor: 'var(--warning)',
        preConfirm: () => {
          const reason = document.getElementById('appealReason').value.trim();
          if (!reason) {
            Swal.showValidationMessage('Reason is required');
            return false;
          }
          return reason;
        }
      }).then(result => {
        if (result.isConfirmed) {
          ajaxPost('/api/appeals/submit.php', { reason: result.value })
            .then(res => {
              if (res.success) {
                showToast('Appeal submitted', 'success');
                location.reload();
              } else {
                showToast(res.message || 'Failed', 'error');
              }
            });
        }
      });
    });
  }

});
```

---

## HTML PAGE TEMPLATE PATTERN

Every customer PHP page must follow this exact pattern:

```php
<?php
// Page-specific variables
$page_title = 'Dashboard'; // Changes per page
$page_css = 'css/dashboard.css'; // Changes per page
$page_js = 'js/dashboard.js'; // Changes per page

// Auth
require_once __DIR__ . '/../includes/auth_check.php';
require_role([ROLE_CUSTOMER]);

// Page-specific PHP logic (DB queries, data preparation)
// ...

// Logger
logger_function_entry(['page' => 'customer/dashboard']);
?>
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en" data-theme="<?= $_SESSION['dark_mode'] ? 'dark' : 'light' ?>"
  style="--primary: <?= get_setting('primary_color') ?>; --secondary: <?= get_setting('secondary_color') ?>; --accent: <?= get_setting('accent_color') ?>; --surface: <?= ($_SESSION['dark_mode'] ? '#1A1A2E' : get_setting('surface_color')) ?>;">
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8">
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
  <title><?= $page_title ?> — <?= get_setting('station_name') ?></title>

  <!-- Google Fonts -->
  <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@300;400;500;600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
  <!-- Material Icons -->
  <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/icon?family=Material+Icons" rel="stylesheet">
  <!-- SweetAlert2 CSS -->
  <link href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/sweetalert2@11/dist/sweetalert2.min.css" rel="stylesheet">

  <!-- Global CSS -->
  <link rel="stylesheet" href="/assets/css/global.css">
  <link rel="stylesheet" href="/assets/css/layout.css">
  <link rel="stylesheet" href="/assets/css/components.css">

  <!-- Page-specific CSS -->
  <link rel="stylesheet" href="<?= $page_css ?>">

  <!-- CSRF Token Meta -->
  <meta name="csrf-token" content="<?= $_SESSION[CSRF_TOKEN_NAME] ?>">
</head>
<body>

  <?php include __DIR__ . '/../includes/header.php'; ?>

  <div class="app-wrapper">
    <?php include __DIR__ . '/../includes/sidebar.php'; ?>

    <div class="main-content">
      <!-- PAGE CONTENT GOES HERE -->
    </div>
  </div>

  <!-- Global JS -->
  <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/sweetalert2@11"></script>
  <script src="/assets/js/global.js"></script>
  <script src="/assets/js/components.js"></script>
  <script src="/assets/js/sidebar.js"></script>

  <!-- Page-specific JS -->
  <script src="<?= $page_js ?>"></script>

  <?php
  logger_function_exit(['page' => 'customer/dashboard']);
  ?>
</body>
</html>
```

**Apply this pattern to ALL 5 customer PHP pages.** Adjust `$page_title`, `$page_css`, `$page_js`, the `require_role()`, the PHP logic section, and the HTML content section accordingly.

## IMPORTANT IMPLEMENTATION NOTES FOR CUSTOMER PAGES

1. **Account Status Handling on Every Page:**
   - If `$_SESSION['status'] === 'pending'`: Show the "Account Pending Approval" notice. Hide or disable all functional content. Only Settings page should be partially accessible (profile viewing).
   - If `$_SESSION['status'] === 'flagged'`: Show the "Account Flagged" warning on dashboard. Allow viewing orders and history. Block "Place Order" page (redirect to dashboard with toast message). Allow Settings access including appeal submission.
   - If `$_SESSION['status'] === 'active'`: Full access to everything.

2. **Every page must use the shared `ajaxPost()` and `ajaxGet()` helper functions** from `global.js` which automatically attach the CSRF token.

3. **Every table must implement pagination** showing max 50 items per page with Previous/Next buttons and a "Showing X-Y of Z items" counter.

4. **All date/time values** displayed to the user must be formatted in Philippines Manila timezone using the helper functions.

5. **Item icons** in tables and cards: If the item has an `item_icon` path, show that image. If NULL/empty, show `/assets/images/default-item.png`.

6. **Status badges** must use the corresponding CSS class: `badge-pending`, `badge-confirmed`, etc. Use the `get_status_badge_class()` PHP function server-side or the JS `formatStatus()` function client-side.

7. **The "Reorder" feature** works by redirecting to `place_order.php?reorder={order_id}`. On that page, PHP fetches the original order's items via `api/orders/reorder.php` and passes them to JS as a JSON variable. JS then pre-selects those items in the grid after items load.

8. **The "View Receipt" button** opens `receipt.php?token={receipt_token}` in a new tab. This is a public page that was built in Prompt #1.

9. **Dark mode** is already handled by the global CSS variables and the `data-theme` attribute on `<html>`. No additional dark mode code is needed in page-specific CSS — just use CSS variables (`var(--text-primary)`, `var(--surface)`, etc.) for all colors.

10. **The sidebar active state** is handled by `sidebar.js` which matches the current URL path to sidebar link hrefs. Each sidebar link should point to the correct relative path (e.g., `dashboard.php`, `place_order.php`, etc.).

11. **Floating label animation** for inputs: The `float-input-group` component has CSS that moves the label up when the input is focused or has a value. Use `placeholder=" "` (a space) on inputs to trigger the `:not(:placeholder-shown)` CSS selector for the filled state.

12. **Glass card effect** should be used sparingly — primarily for main content cards like settings sections, stat cards, and the dashboard pending/flagged notices. Not on every element.

13. **All customer-facing tables** should show human-readable values: "Cash on Delivery" instead of "cod", "On Delivery" instead of "on_delivery", etc. Use mapping objects in JS.

14. **Each page-specific JS file** must be wrapped in `document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() { ... })` to ensure DOM is ready.

15. **Error handling**: Every AJAX call must have `.catch()` that shows a toast with a generic error message. Never leave failed requests silently unhandled.

You are continuing the build of **"Azeu Water Station"** — a Philippine-based Water Refilling Station management web application. ## PROJECT CONTEXT RECAP

Azeu Water Station is a web-based order and delivery management system for a water refilling station in the Philippines. It has 4 roles: Customer, Rider, Staff, Admin (with Super Admin). The tech stack is pure PHP (no frameworks), MySQL on XAMPP (database name: `station_azeu`), and hand-written HTML/CSS/JS. No frameworks, no Bootstrap, no Tailwind.

**Riders** are delivery personnel who:
- Cannot register themselves — accounts are created by Staff or Admin only
- Are always `status='active'` from creation (skip pending approval since created by authority)
- View deliveries assigned to them by Staff/Admin
- Organize their delivery priority order via drag-and-drop
- Set themselves as Available or Unavailable (but cannot go Unavailable while having `on_delivery` orders)
- Mark orders as `On Delivery` (which auto-sets `expected_delivery_date` to today)
- Mark orders as `Delivered` (which sets `delivered_at` timestamp and counts to store income)
- Can cancel assigned deliveries with a reason (order reverts to `Confirmed` status with `rider_id` set to NULL for Staff to reassign)
- View their delivery history (completed and cancelled)
- Manage their own profile and password in Settings

---

## ORDER LIFECYCLE (Rider Perspective)

### What the Rider Sees

Riders only see orders that are **assigned to them** (`rider_id = their user ID`). They do NOT see pending or confirmed orders — those are managed by Staff/Admin. Once Staff/Admin assigns a rider to an order, it appears in the rider's "Assigned Deliveries" page.

### Status Transitions a Rider Can Make

```
ASSIGNED ──► ON DELIVERY ──► DELIVERED
    │              │
    │              └── Cancel (with reason) → reverts to CONFIRMED, rider_id = NULL
    └── Cancel (with reason) → reverts to CONFIRMED, rider_id = NULL
```

**Rider actions:**
1. **Mark as On Delivery** — Changes status from `assigned` to `on_delivery`. This automatically sets `expected_delivery_date` to today's date. This means the rider has picked up the items from the station and is on the way to the customer. **Once a rider marks ANY order as On Delivery, they CANNOT set themselves as Unavailable until ALL their on_delivery orders are completed (delivered) or cancelled.**

2. **Mark as Delivered** — Changes status from `on_delivery` to `delivered`. This sets `delivered_at` to NOW(). The order amount is now counted toward store income. A notification is sent to the customer: "Order #{id} has been delivered!"

3. **Cancel Delivery** — Rider can cancel at `assigned` or `on_delivery` status. A reason is REQUIRED. When a rider cancels:
   - The order status reverts to `confirmed` (NOT cancelled — the order still exists)
   - `rider_id` is set to NULL (unassigned)
   - Staff/Admin can then reassign to another rider
   - If the order was `on_delivery`, stock is NOT restored (stock was decremented at confirmation, and the order is still going to be fulfilled — just by a different rider)
   - A notification is sent to Staff/Admin: "Rider {name} cancelled delivery of Order #{id}. Reason: {reason}"
   - This is treated as a rider reassignment request, NOT as an order cancellation

### Delivery Priority System

Riders can reorder their assigned deliveries to plan their route. This is a drag-and-drop feature:

- Each assigned/on_delivery order has a priority number stored in `delivery_priority` table
- Lower `priority_order` number = deliver first (higher priority)
- Default priority is set when the order is assigned (based on assignment order — first assigned = priority 1, etc.)
- Rider can drag-and-drop to reorder on the `assigned_deliveries.php` page
- On reorder, JS sends the new priority list to `api/riders/update_priority.php`
- The table/list displays orders sorted by `priority_order ASC`
- Only `assigned` and `on_delivery` orders are in the priority list (not delivered/cancelled)

### Rider Availability System

- `is_available` column in `users` table (TINYINT: 0 or 1)
- Default: 1 (available) when account is created
- Rider can toggle via a switch on their dashboard
- **Restriction:** Cannot set to Unavailable (0) if they have ANY orders with status `on_delivery`. They must complete or cancel all on_delivery orders first. The API endpoint enforces this — returns an error if rider tries to go unavailable while having on_delivery orders.
- When `is_available = 0`: The rider will NOT be selected by the auto-assign algorithm. Staff/Admin CAN still manually assign orders to unavailable riders (but will see a warning).
- The availability status is shown on the rider's dashboard and in Staff/Admin rider statistics pages.

## PAGE-BY-PAGE SPECIFICATIONS

---

### 1. `rider/dashboard.php`

**PHP Logic (top of file):**
```
1. Include auth_check.php, require_role([ROLE_RIDER])
2. Get current user data from session
3. Fetch rider's current availability status from DB (fresh read, not session cache):
   SELECT is_available FROM users WHERE id = session.user_id
4. Fetch dashboard stats:
   - Assigned deliveries count:
     SELECT COUNT(*) FROM orders WHERE rider_id = user_id AND status IN ('assigned', 'on_delivery')
   - On delivery count:
     SELECT COUNT(*) FROM orders WHERE rider_id = user_id AND status = 'on_delivery'
   - Completed today count:
     SELECT COUNT(*) FROM orders WHERE rider_id = user_id AND status = 'delivered'
     AND DATE(delivered_at) = CURDATE()
5. Check if rider can toggle availability:
   $has_on_delivery = (on_delivery_count > 0)
   → If true, the toggle switch should be locked to "Available" and cannot be turned off
6. Fetch delivery preview (max 3, sorted by priority):
   SELECT o.*, GROUP_CONCAT(oi.item_name) as item_names,
   u.full_name as customer_name, u.phone as customer_phone,
   ca.full_address as customer_address,
   dp.priority_order
   FROM orders o
   LEFT JOIN order_items oi ON o.id = oi.order_id
   LEFT JOIN users u ON o.customer_id = u.id
   LEFT JOIN customer_addresses ca ON (ca.customer_id = o.customer_id AND ca.is_default = 1)
   LEFT JOIN delivery_priority dp ON (dp.order_id = o.id AND dp.rider_id = o.rider_id)
   WHERE o.rider_id = session.user_id AND o.status IN ('assigned', 'on_delivery')
   GROUP BY o.id
   ORDER BY dp.priority_order ASC, o.created_at ASC
   LIMIT 3
7. Include header.php, sidebar.php
```

**HTML Structure:**
```html
<div class="main-content">
  <div class="page-header">
    <h1>Dashboard</h1>
  </div>

  <!-- Greeting + Availability Toggle Row -->

    <div class="greeting">
      <h2>Welcome back, {Full Name}! 👋</h2>
      <p class="text-muted">Here's your delivery overview for today.</p>
    </div>

    <!-- Availability Toggle -->
    <div class="availability-toggle glass-card">
      <div class="availability-info">
        <span class="material-icons availability-icon {available ? 'text-success' : 'text-danger'}">
          {available ? 'check_circle' : 'cancel'}
        </span>
        <div>
          <span class="availability-label">
            {available ? 'Available' : 'Unavailable'}
          </span>
          <small class="text-muted">
            {available ? 'You can receive new deliveries' : 'You will not receive new deliveries'}
          </small>
        </div>
      </div>
      <label class="toggle-switch">
        <input type="checkbox" id="availabilityToggle"
               {if is_available: checked}
               {if has_on_delivery: disabled title="Cannot go unavailable while on delivery"}>
        <span class="toggle-slider"></span>
      </label>
      {if has_on_delivery:
        <small class="text-warning toggle-warning">
          <span class="material-icons" style="font-size:14px;vertical-align:middle;">warning</span>
          Complete active deliveries before going unavailable
        </small>
      }
    </div>
  </div>

  <!-- Quick Action Buttons -->
  <div class="quick-actions">
    <a href="assigned_deliveries.php" class="quick-action-btn">
      <span class="material-icons">local_shipping</span>
      <span>Assigned Deliveries</span>
    </a>
    <a href="delivery_history.php" class="quick-action-btn">

    </a>
  </div>

  <!-- Stat Cards -->

      <div class="stat-icon" style="background: var(--teal)">
        <span class="material-icons">delivery_dining</span>
      </div>
      <div class="stat-info">
        <span class="stat-number">{on_delivery_count}</span>
        <span class="stat-label">On Delivery</span>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="stat-card">
      <div class="stat-icon" style="background: var(--success)">
        <span class="material-icons">task_alt</span>
      </div>
      <div class="stat-info">
        <span class="stat-number">{completed_today}</span>
        <span class="stat-label">Completed Today</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

  <!-- Delivery Preview Section -->
  <div class="preview-section">
    <div class="preview-header">
      <h3>Upcoming Deliveries</h3>

      <span class="material-icons">inbox</span>

    </div>

    <!-- IF DELIVERIES EXIST -->

          </tr>
        </tbody>
      </table>
    </div>
  </div>

</div>
```

### `rider/css/dashboard.css`

```
.stat-card:
  - Glass card effect, flex row, align center, gap 16px, padding 20px
  - .stat-icon: 48x48px circle, flex center, border-radius 50%, color white
  - .stat-number: font-size 1.8em, font-weight 700, line-height 1
  - .stat-label: font-size 0.85em, color var(--text-muted), margin-top 2px

.preview-section:
  - Glass card, padding 20px
  - .preview-header: flex row, space-between, align center, margin-bottom 16px

.priority-number:
  - Display inline-flex, align center, justify center
  - 28x28px circle, background var(--primary), color white, font-weight 700, font-size 0.85em
  - Border-radius 50%

.customer-details-cell:
  - Line-height 1.5
  - strong: display block
  - small: word-break break-word, max-width 250px

.item-with-icon:
  - Flex inline, align center, gap 6px
  - .item-icon-sm: 24x24px, border-radius 4px, object-fit cover

.empty-state (from components.css extended):
  - Flex column, align center, justify center, padding 40px
  - Icon: font-size 48px, color var(--text-muted), margin-bottom 12px
  - p: font-size 1em, color var(--text-secondary)
  - small: margin-top 4px

Responsive:
  @media (max-width: 1024px):
    - dashboard-top: flex column
    - availability-toggle: full width
  @media (max-width: 768px):
    - stats-grid: 1 column
    - quick-actions: flex wrap, buttons smaller
    - table: horizontal scroll
  @media (max-width: 480px):
    - customer-details-cell max-width: unset
```

### `rider/js/dashboard.js`

```javascript
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {

  // ===== AVAILABILITY TOGGLE =====
  const toggleInput = document.getElementById('availabilityToggle');
  if (toggleInput && !toggleInput.disabled) {
    toggleInput.addEventListener('change', function() {
      const newState = this.checked; // true = available, false = unavailable
      const confirmMsg = newState
        ? 'Set yourself as Available? You may receive new delivery assignments.'
        : 'Set yourself as Unavailable? You will not receive new delivery assignments.';

      Swal.fire({
        title: newState ? 'Go Available?' : 'Go Unavailable?',
        text: confirmMsg,
        icon: 'question',
        showCancelButton: true,
        confirmButtonText: newState ? 'Yes, Go Available' : 'Yes, Go Unavailable',
        cancelButtonText: 'Cancel',
        confirmButtonColor: newState ? 'var(--success)' : 'var(--warning)',
      }).then(result => {
        if (result.isConfirmed) {
          ajaxPost('/api/riders/toggle_availability.php', {})
            .then(data => {
              if (data.success) {
                showToast(
                  newState ? 'You are now available for deliveries' : 'You are now unavailable',
                  'success'
                );
                // Update visual state
                updateAvailabilityUI(newState);
              } else {
                // Revert toggle
                toggleInput.checked = !newState;
                showToast(data.message || 'Failed to update availability', 'error');
              }
            })
            .catch(err => {
              toggleInput.checked = !newState;
              showToast('An error occurred. Please try again.', 'error');
            });
        } else {
          // User cancelled the dialog — revert the toggle
          toggleInput.checked = !newState;
        }
      });
    });
  }

  function updateAvailabilityUI(isAvailable) {
    const icon = document.querySelector('.availability-icon');
    const label = document.querySelector('.availability-label');
    const sublabel = icon.closest('.availability-info').querySelector('small');

    if (isAvailable) {
      icon.textContent = 'check_circle';
      icon.classList.remove('text-danger');
      icon.classList.add('text-success');
      label.textContent = 'Available';
      sublabel.textContent = 'You can receive new deliveries';
    } else {
      icon.textContent = 'cancel';
      icon.classList.remove('text-success');
      icon.classList.add('text-danger');
      label.textContent = 'Unavailable';
      sublabel.textContent = 'You will not receive new deliveries';
    }
  }

  // Dashboard stats and preview are rendered server-side by PHP
  // No additional AJAX needed on dashboard page load

});
```

---

### 2. `rider/assigned_deliveries.php`

This is the rider's main working page. It shows all currently assigned and on-delivery orders, allows status changes, cancellation, and drag-and-drop reordering.

**PHP Logic (top of file):**
```
1. Include auth_check.php, require_role([ROLE_RIDER])
2. Get rider's current availability from DB
3. Include header.php, sidebar.php
4. NOTE: Order data is loaded via AJAX (JS handles fetching and rendering)
   But we need the rider_id for the API calls — it comes from session.
```

**HTML Structure:**
```html
<div class="main-content">
  <div class="page-header">
    <div class="page-header-left">
      <h1>Assigned Deliveries</h1>
      <p class="text-muted">Manage and track your current deliveries.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="page-header-right">
      <!-- Availability status indicator (small, in header) -->
      <div class="availability-badge {is_available ? 'available' : 'unavailable'}">
        <span class="material-icons">{is_available ? 'check_circle' : 'cancel'}</span>
        <span>{is_available ? 'Available' : 'Unavailable'}</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

  <!-- Filter Bar -->
  <div class="filter-bar" id="deliveryFilters">
    <button class="filter-btn active" data-filter="all">All</button>
    <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="assigned">Assigned</button>
    <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="on_delivery">On Delivery</button>
  </div>

  <!-- Bulk Actions Bar -->
  <div class="bulk-actions-bar" id="bulkActions" style="display: none;">
    <span id="bulkSelectedCount">0</span> delivery(ies) selected
    <button class="btn btn-success btn-sm" id="bulkOnDeliveryBtn" title="Mark selected as On Delivery">
      <span class="material-icons">local_shipping</span> Mark On Delivery

    </button>
  </div>

  <!-- Deliveries Table (sortable via drag-and-drop) -->
  <div class="data-table-wrapper">
    <table class="data-table" id="deliveriesTable">
      <thead>
        <tr>
          <th style="width:40px;">
            <input type="checkbox" class="custom-checkbox" id="selectAllDeliveries">
          </th>
          <th style="width:40px;" title="Drag to reorder priority">
            <span class="material-icons" style="font-size:18px;">drag_indicator</span>
          </th>
          <th style="width:50px;">Priority</th>
          <th>Order ID</th>
          <th>Customer Details</th>

          <td colspan="13"><div class="spinner"></div></td>
        </tr>
      </tbody>
    </table>
  </div>

  <!-- Pagination -->
  <div class="pagination" id="deliveriesPagination"></div>

  <!-- Empty State -->
  <div class="empty-state" id="emptyDeliveries" style="display: none;">
    <span class="material-icons">local_shipping</span>
    <p>No deliveries assigned to you.</p>
    <small class="text-muted">New deliveries will appear here when staff assigns them.</small>
  </div>
</div>
```

### `rider/css/assigned_deliveries.css`

```
.page-header:

  - Flex row, gap 4px

    - Or keep draggable but with touch support (Sortable.js handles this)
```
