### `rider/js/assigned_deliveries.js`

This is the most complex rider JS file.

```javascript
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {

  let currentFilter = 'all';
  let currentPage = 1;
  const perPage = 50;
  let sortableInstance = null;

  // Load deliveries on page load
  loadDeliveries();

  // ===== FILTER BUTTONS =====
  document.querySelectorAll('#deliveryFilters .filter-btn').forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      document.querySelectorAll('#deliveryFilters .filter-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
      this.classList.add('active');
      currentFilter = this.dataset.filter;
      currentPage = 1;
      loadDeliveries();
    });
  });

  // ===== LOAD DELIVERIES =====
  function loadDeliveries() {
    const params = {
      status: currentFilter === 'all' ? 'assigned,on_delivery' : currentFilter,
      page: currentPage,
      scope: 'active' // Tell API to return only assigned + on_delivery for rider
    };

    document.getElementById('deliveriesBody').innerHTML =
      '<tr class="loading-row"><td colspan="13"><div class="spinner"></div></td></tr>';
    document.getElementById('emptyDeliveries').style.display = 'none';

    ajaxGet('/api/orders/get_orders.php', params)
      .then(data => {
        if (!data.orders || data.orders.length === 0) {
          document.getElementById('deliveriesBody').innerHTML = '';
          document.getElementById('emptyDeliveries').style.display = 'flex';
          document.getElementById('deliveriesPagination').innerHTML = '';
          destroySortable();
          return;
        }

        document.getElementById('emptyDeliveries').style.display = 'none';
        renderDeliveries(data.orders);
        renderPagination(data.total, data.page, data.per_page);
        initSortable();
      })
      .catch(err => {
        showToast('Failed to load deliveries', 'error');
      });
  }

  // ===== RENDER DELIVERIES TABLE =====
  function renderDeliveries(orders) {
    const tbody = document.getElementById('deliveriesBody');
    tbody.innerHTML = '';

    const paymentLabels = { cod: 'Cash on Delivery', pickup: 'Pickup at Store', online: 'Online' };

    orders.forEach((order, index) => {
      const tr = document.createElement('tr');
      tr.dataset.orderId = order.id;
      tr.dataset.status = order.status;

      // Items display
      const itemsHtml = order.items.map(item =>
        `<span class="item-with-icon">
          <img src="${item.item_icon || '/assets/images/default-item.png'}" class="item-icon-sm">
          ${item.item_name}
        </span>`
      ).join('<br>');

      // Total quantity
      const totalQty = order.items.reduce((sum, i) => sum + parseInt(i.quantity), 0);

      // Customer details formatted:
      // "Customer Name"
      // "📞 Phone Number"
      // "📍 Full Address"
      const customerDetails = `
        <strong>${order.customer_name || 'Unknown'}</strong>
        <span class="customer-phone">
          <span class="material-icons" style="font-size:14px;vertical-align:middle;">phone</span>
          ${order.customer_phone || 'N/A'}
        </span>
        <small class="customer-address">
          <span class="material-icons" style="font-size:14px;vertical-align:middle;">location_on</span>
          ${order.delivery_address || order.customer_default_address || 'No address'}
        </small>
      `;

      // Determine available actions based on status
      let actionsHtml = '';

      if (order.status === 'assigned') {
        actionsHtml = `
          <button class="btn-icon btn-success" title="Mark On Delivery"
                  onclick="markOnDelivery(${order.id})">
            <span class="material-icons">local_shipping</span>
          </button>
          <button class="btn-icon btn-danger" title="Cancel Delivery"
                  onclick="cancelDelivery(${order.id})">
            <span class="material-icons">cancel</span>
          </button>
        `;
      } else if (order.status === 'on_delivery') {
        actionsHtml = `
          <button class="btn-icon btn-primary" title="Mark Delivered"
                  onclick="markDelivered(${order.id})">
            <span class="material-icons">check_circle</span>
          </button>
          <button class="btn-icon btn-danger" title="Cancel Delivery"
                  onclick="cancelDelivery(${order.id})">
            <span class="material-icons">cancel</span>
          </button>
        `;
      }

      tr.innerHTML = `
        <td>
          <input type="checkbox" class="custom-checkbox delivery-checkbox" data-order-id="${order.id}">
        </td>
        <td class="drag-handle-cell">
          <span class="material-icons drag-handle">drag_indicator</span>
        </td>
        <td>
          <span class="priority-number">${order.priority_order || (index + 1)}</span>
        </td>
        <td><strong>#${order.id}</strong></td>
        <td class="customer-details-cell">${customerDetails}</td>
        <td class="items-cell">${itemsHtml}</td>
        <td>${totalQty}</td>
        <td>${paymentLabels[order.payment_type] || order.payment_type}</td>
        <td><span class="badge badge-${order.status.replace(/_/g, '-')}">${formatStatus(order.status)}</span></td>
        <td>${formatDate(order.order_date)}</td>
        <td>${order.expected_delivery_date ? formatDate(order.expected_delivery_date) : '<span class="text-muted">—</span>'}</td>
        <td class="notes-cell" title="${escapeHtml(order.order_notes || '')}">${order.order_notes || '<span class="text-muted">—</span>'}</td>
        <td class="actions-cell">${actionsHtml}</td>
      `;

      tbody.appendChild(tr);
    });
  }

  // ===== SORTABLE.JS — Drag-and-Drop Priority =====
  function initSortable() {
    destroySortable(); // Destroy any existing instance first

    const tbody = document.getElementById('deliveriesBody');
    sortableInstance = new Sortable(tbody, {
      handle: '.drag-handle',       // Only drag from the handle icon
      animation: 200,               // Smooth animation duration
      ghostClass: 'sortable-ghost', // Class on the drop placeholder
      chosenClass: 'sortable-chosen', // Class on the chosen item
      dragClass: 'sortable-drag',   // Class on the dragging item
      onEnd: function(evt) {
        // After drag-and-drop, save new priority order
        savePriorityOrder();
      }
    });
  }

  function destroySortable() {
    if (sortableInstance) {
      sortableInstance.destroy();
      sortableInstance = null;
    }
  }

  function savePriorityOrder() {
    const rows = document.querySelectorAll('#deliveriesBody tr[data-order-id]');
    const priorities = [];

    rows.forEach((row, index) => {
      const orderId = parseInt(row.dataset.orderId);
      const newPriority = index + 1;
      priorities.push({ order_id: orderId, priority_order: newPriority });

      // Update the visual priority number
      const prioritySpan = row.querySelector('.priority-number');
      if (prioritySpan) prioritySpan.textContent = newPriority;
    });

    // Send new priority order to server
    ajaxPost('/api/riders/update_priority.php', {
      priorities: JSON.stringify(priorities)
    }).then(data => {
      if (data.success) {
        showToast('Delivery priority updated', 'success');
      } else {
        showToast(data.message || 'Failed to update priority', 'error');
        loadDeliveries(); // Reload to revert
      }
    }).catch(err => {
      showToast('Failed to save priority order', 'error');
      loadDeliveries();
    });
  }

  // ===== ACTION: Mark On Delivery =====
  window.markOnDelivery = function(orderId) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Mark as On Delivery?',
      html: `
        <p>Confirm that you have picked up the items and are on the way to deliver <strong>Order #${orderId}</strong>.</p>
        <p style="margin-top:8px;color:var(--text-muted);font-size:0.9em;">
          <span class="material-icons" style="font-size:16px;vertical-align:middle;">info</span>
          Expected delivery date will be set to today.
        </p>
        <p style="margin-top:4px;color:var(--warning);font-size:0.85em;">
          <span class="material-icons" style="font-size:16px;vertical-align:middle;">warning</span>
          You cannot go unavailable while you have active deliveries.
        </p>
      `,
      icon: 'question',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Yes, On Delivery',
      cancelButtonText: 'Not Yet',
      confirmButtonColor: 'var(--teal)'
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/orders/update_status.php', {
          order_id: orderId,
          new_status: 'on_delivery'
        }).then(data => {
          if (data.success) {
            showToast('Order marked as On Delivery', 'success');
            loadDeliveries();
          } else {
            showToast(data.message || 'Failed to update status', 'error');
          }
        }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  };

  // ===== ACTION: Mark Delivered =====
  window.markDelivered = function(orderId) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Mark as Delivered?',
      html: `
        <p>Confirm that <strong>Order #${orderId}</strong> has been successfully delivered to the customer.</p>
        <p style="margin-top:8px;color:var(--text-muted);font-size:0.9em;">
          This action cannot be undone.
        </p>
      `,
      icon: 'question',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Yes, Delivered',
      cancelButtonText: 'Not Yet',
      confirmButtonColor: 'var(--success)'
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/orders/update_status.php', {
          order_id: orderId,
          new_status: 'delivered'
        }).then(data => {
          if (data.success) {
            showToast('Order marked as Delivered!', 'success');
            loadDeliveries(); // This will remove the delivered order from active list
          } else {
            showToast(data.message || 'Failed to update status', 'error');
          }
        }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  };

  // ===== ACTION: Cancel Delivery =====
  window.cancelDelivery = function(orderId) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Cancel Delivery?',
      html: `
        <p>Cancel your delivery of <strong>Order #${orderId}</strong>?</p>
        <p style="margin-top:4px;color:var(--text-muted);font-size:0.9em;">
          The order will be sent back to staff for reassignment to another rider.
        </p>
        <textarea id="cancelReason" class="swal2-textarea"
          placeholder="Reason for cancellation (required)" rows="3"
          style="margin-top:12px;"></textarea>
      `,
      icon: 'warning',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Yes, Cancel Delivery',
      cancelButtonText: 'Keep It',
      confirmButtonColor: '#EF5350',
      preConfirm: () => {
        const reason = document.getElementById('cancelReason').value.trim();
        if (!reason) {
          Swal.showValidationMessage('Please provide a reason for cancellation');
          return false;
        }
        return reason;
      }
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/orders/cancel_order.php', {
          order_id: orderId,
          reason: result.value
        }).then(data => {
          if (data.success) {
            showToast('Delivery cancelled. Order sent back for reassignment.', 'info');
            loadDeliveries();
          } else {
            showToast(data.message || 'Failed to cancel delivery', 'error');
          }
        }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  };

  // ===== BULK ACTIONS =====

  // Select All checkbox
  document.getElementById('selectAllDeliveries').addEventListener('change', function() {
    const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.delivery-checkbox');
    checkboxes.forEach(cb => { cb.checked = this.checked; });
    updateBulkBar();
  });

  // Individual checkbox change (delegated)
  document.getElementById('deliveriesBody').addEventListener('change', function(e) {
    if (e.target.classList.contains('delivery-checkbox')) {
      updateBulkBar();
    }
  });

  function updateBulkBar() {
    const checked = document.querySelectorAll('.delivery-checkbox:checked').length;
    const bar = document.getElementById('bulkActions');
    bar.style.display = checked > 0 ? 'flex' : 'none';
    document.getElementById('bulkSelectedCount').textContent = checked;
  }

  function getSelectedOrderIds() {
    const ids = [];
    document.querySelectorAll('.delivery-checkbox:checked').forEach(cb => {
      ids.push(parseInt(cb.dataset.orderId));
    });
    return ids;
  }

  // Bulk Mark On Delivery
  document.getElementById('bulkOnDeliveryBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
    const ids = getSelectedOrderIds();
    if (ids.length === 0) return;

    Swal.fire({
      title: `Mark ${ids.length} Order(s) as On Delivery?`,
      text: 'All selected assigned orders will be marked as On Delivery.',
      icon: 'question',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Yes, Mark All',
      confirmButtonColor: 'var(--teal)'
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/orders/bulk_update.php', {
          order_ids: JSON.stringify(ids),
          action: 'on_delivery'
        }).then(data => {
          showToast(`${data.success || 0} order(s) marked as On Delivery`, 'success');
          if (data.failed > 0) {
            showToast(`${data.failed} order(s) could not be updated`, 'warning');
          }
          loadDeliveries();
        }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  });

  // Bulk Mark Delivered
  document.getElementById('bulkDeliveredBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
    const ids = getSelectedOrderIds();
    if (ids.length === 0) return;

    Swal.fire({
      title: `Mark ${ids.length} Order(s) as Delivered?`,
      text: 'All selected on-delivery orders will be marked as Delivered. This cannot be undone.',
      icon: 'question',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Yes, Mark All Delivered',
      confirmButtonColor: 'var(--success)'
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/orders/bulk_update.php', {
          order_ids: JSON.stringify(ids),
          action: 'delivered'
        }).then(data => {
          showToast(`${data.success || 0} order(s) marked as Delivered`, 'success');
          if (data.failed > 0) {
            showToast(`${data.failed} order(s) could not be updated`, 'warning');
          }
          loadDeliveries();
        }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  });

  // Bulk Cancel
  document.getElementById('bulkCancelBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
    const ids = getSelectedOrderIds();
    if (ids.length === 0) return;

    Swal.fire({
      title: `Cancel ${ids.length} Delivery(ies)?`,
      html: `
        <p>Selected orders will be sent back to staff for reassignment.</p>
        <textarea id="bulkCancelReason" class="swal2-textarea"
          placeholder="Reason for cancellation (required)" rows="3"></textarea>
      `,
      icon: 'warning',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Yes, Cancel All',
      confirmButtonColor: '#EF5350',
      preConfirm: () => {
        const reason = document.getElementById('bulkCancelReason').value.trim();
        if (!reason) {
          Swal.showValidationMessage('Please provide a reason');
          return false;
        }
        return reason;
      }
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/orders/bulk_update.php', {
          order_ids: JSON.stringify(ids),
          action: 'cancel',
          reason: result.value
        }).then(data => {
          showToast(`${data.success || 0} delivery(ies) cancelled`, 'info');
          loadDeliveries();
        }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  });

  // ===== HELPER FUNCTIONS =====
  function formatStatus(status) {
    const labels = {
      pending: 'Pending', confirmed: 'Confirmed', assigned: 'Assigned',
      on_delivery: 'On Delivery', delivered: 'Delivered', accepted: 'Accepted',
      ready_for_pickup: 'Ready for Pickup', picked_up: 'Picked Up', cancelled: 'Cancelled'
    };
    return labels[status] || status;
  }

  function formatDate(dateStr) {
    if (!dateStr) return '—';
    const d = new Date(dateStr);
    return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 'numeric', year: 'numeric' })
      + ' ' + d.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
  }

  function escapeHtml(text) {
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.textContent = text;
    return div.innerHTML;
  }

  function renderPagination(total, page, perPage) {
    const totalPages = Math.ceil(total / perPage);
    const container = document.getElementById('deliveriesPagination');
    container.innerHTML = '';
    if (totalPages <= 1) return;

    const prevBtn = document.createElement('button');
    prevBtn.className = 'page-btn';
    prevBtn.textContent = 'Previous';
    prevBtn.disabled = page <= 1;
    prevBtn.addEventListener('click', () => { currentPage--; loadDeliveries(); });
    container.appendChild(prevBtn);

    for (let i = Math.max(1, page - 2); i <= Math.min(totalPages, page + 2); i++) {
      const pb = document.createElement('button');
      pb.className = `page-btn ${i === page ? 'active' : ''}`;
      pb.textContent = i;
      pb.addEventListener('click', () => { currentPage = i; loadDeliveries(); });
      container.appendChild(pb);
    }

    const nextBtn = document.createElement('button');
    nextBtn.className = 'page-btn';
    nextBtn.textContent = 'Next';
    nextBtn.disabled = page >= totalPages;
    nextBtn.addEventListener('click', () => { currentPage++; loadDeliveries(); });
    container.appendChild(nextBtn);

    const info = document.createElement('span');
    info.className = 'pagination-info';
    info.textContent = `Showing ${(page - 1) * perPage + 1}–${Math.min(page * perPage, total)} of ${total} deliveries`;
    container.appendChild(info);
  }

});
```

```html
<div class="main-content">
```

### `rider/js/delivery_history.js`

```javascript
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {

  let currentFilter = 'all';
  let currentPage = 1;
  let searchText = '';
  let dateFrom = '';
  let dateTo = '';
  const perPage = 50;

  // Load stats and history on page load
  loadStats();
  loadHistory();

  // ===== PERFORMANCE STATS =====
  function loadStats() {
    // Fetch rider-specific stats
    ajaxGet('/api/riders/get_statistics.php', { self: true })
      .then(data => {
        document.getElementById('totalDelivered').textContent = data.completed || 0;
        document.getElementById('totalCancelled').textContent = data.cancelled || 0;
        const rate = data.completed > 0
          ? ((data.completed / (data.completed + data.cancelled)) * 100).toFixed(1)
          : '0.0';
        document.getElementById('successRate').textContent = rate + '%';
      })
      .catch(() => {
        document.getElementById('totalDelivered').textContent = '—';
        document.getElementById('totalCancelled').textContent = '—';
        document.getElementById('successRate').textContent = '—';
      });
  }

  // ===== FILTER BUTTONS =====
  document.querySelectorAll('#historyFilters .filter-btn').forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      document.querySelectorAll('#historyFilters .filter-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
      this.classList.add('active');
      currentFilter = this.dataset.filter;
      currentPage = 1;
      loadHistory();
    });
  });

  // ===== SEARCH (debounced) =====
  let searchTimeout;
  document.getElementById('historySearch').addEventListener('input', function() {
    clearTimeout(searchTimeout);
    searchTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
      searchText = this.value.trim();
      currentPage = 1;
      loadHistory();
    }, 300);
  });

  // ===== DATE RANGE =====
  document.getElementById('dateFrom').addEventListener('change', function() {
    dateFrom = this.value;
    currentPage = 1;
    loadHistory();
  });
  document.getElementById('dateTo').addEventListener('change', function() {
    dateTo = this.value;
    currentPage = 1;
    loadHistory();
  });

  // ===== LOAD HISTORY =====
  function loadHistory() {
    const statusFilter = currentFilter === 'all' ? 'delivered,cancelled' : currentFilter;

    const params = {
      status: statusFilter,
      search: searchText,
      page: currentPage,
      date_from: dateFrom,
      date_to: dateTo,
      scope: 'history' // Tell API to return completed/cancelled orders for rider
    };

    document.getElementById('historyBody').innerHTML =
      '<tr class="loading-row"><td colspan="9"><div class="spinner"></div></td></tr>';
    document.getElementById('emptyHistory').style.display = 'none';

    ajaxGet('/api/orders/get_orders.php', params)
      .then(data => {
        if (!data.orders || data.orders.length === 0) {
          document.getElementById('historyBody').innerHTML = '';
          document.getElementById('emptyHistory').style.display = 'flex';
          document.getElementById('historyPagination').innerHTML = '';
          return;
        }

        document.getElementById('emptyHistory').style.display = 'none';
        renderHistory(data.orders);
        renderPagination(data.total, data.page, data.per_page);
      })
      .catch(() => showToast('Failed to load delivery history', 'error'));
  }

  // ===== RENDER HISTORY TABLE =====
  function renderHistory(orders) {
    const tbody = document.getElementById('historyBody');
    tbody.innerHTML = '';

    const paymentLabels = { cod: 'Cash on Delivery', pickup: 'Pickup at Store', online: 'Online' };

    orders.forEach(order => {
      const tr = document.createElement('tr');

      const itemsHtml = order.items.map(item =>
        `<span class="item-with-icon">
          <img src="${item.item_icon || '/assets/images/default-item.png'}" class="item-icon-sm">
          ${item.item_name}
        </span>`
      ).join('<br>');

      const totalQty = order.items.reduce((sum, i) => sum + parseInt(i.quantity), 0);

      const customerDetails = `
        <strong>${order.customer_name || 'Unknown'}</strong>
        <span class="customer-phone">
          <span class="material-icons" style="font-size:14px;vertical-align:middle;">phone</span>
          ${order.customer_phone || 'N/A'}
        </span>
        <small class="customer-address">
          <span class="material-icons" style="font-size:14px;vertical-align:middle;">location_on</span>
          ${order.delivery_address || order.customer_default_address || 'No address'}
        </small>
      `;

      // For cancelled orders by rider, the cancellation reason is shown
      // Note: When rider cancels, the order reverts to Confirmed — it's not truly "cancelled"
      // But the history might show orders that were later cancelled by staff after rider returned them
      // The API should return the cancellation_reason if status is cancelled
      let cancelReasonHtml = '<span class="text-muted">—</span>';
      if (order.status === 'cancelled' && order.cancellation_reason) {
        cancelReasonHtml = `<span class="truncate-text" title="${escapeHtml(order.cancellation_reason)}">${escapeHtml(order.cancellation_reason)}</span>`;
      }

      tr.innerHTML = `
        <td><strong>#${order.id}</strong></td>
        <td class="customer-details-cell">${customerDetails}</td>
        <td class="items-cell">${itemsHtml}</td>
        <td>${totalQty}</td>
        <td>${paymentLabels[order.payment_type] || order.payment_type}</td>
        <td><span class="badge badge-${order.status.replace(/_/g, '-')}">${formatStatus(order.status)}</span></td>
        <td>${formatDate(order.order_date)}</td>
        <td>${order.delivered_at ? formatDate(order.delivered_at) : '<span class="text-muted">—</span>'}</td>
        <td class="cancellation-cell">${cancelReasonHtml}</td>
      `;

      tbody.appendChild(tr);
    });
  }

  // ===== HELPER FUNCTIONS =====
  function formatStatus(status) {
    const labels = {
      pending: 'Pending', confirmed: 'Confirmed', assigned: 'Assigned',
      on_delivery: 'On Delivery', delivered: 'Delivered', accepted: 'Accepted',
      ready_for_pickup: 'Ready for Pickup', picked_up: 'Picked Up', cancelled: 'Cancelled'
    };
    return labels[status] || status;
  }

  function formatDate(dateStr) {
    if (!dateStr) return '—';
    const d = new Date(dateStr);
    return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 'numeric', year: 'numeric' })
      + ' ' + d.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
  }

  function escapeHtml(text) {
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.textContent = text || '';
    return div.innerHTML;
  }

  function renderPagination(total, page, perPage) {
    const totalPages = Math.ceil(total / perPage);
    const container = document.getElementById('historyPagination');
    container.innerHTML = '';
    if (totalPages <= 1) return;

    const prevBtn = document.createElement('button');
    prevBtn.className = 'page-btn';
    prevBtn.textContent = 'Previous';
    prevBtn.disabled = page <= 1;
    prevBtn.addEventListener('click', () => { currentPage--; loadHistory(); });
    container.appendChild(prevBtn);

    for (let i = Math.max(1, page - 2); i <= Math.min(totalPages, page + 2); i++) {
      const pb = document.createElement('button');
      pb.className = `page-btn ${i === page ? 'active' : ''}`;
      pb.textContent = i;
      pb.addEventListener('click', () => { currentPage = i; loadHistory(); });
      container.appendChild(pb);
    }

    const nextBtn = document.createElement('button');
    nextBtn.className = 'page-btn';
    nextBtn.textContent = 'Next';
    nextBtn.disabled = page >= totalPages;
    nextBtn.addEventListener('click', () => { currentPage++; loadHistory(); });
    container.appendChild(nextBtn);

    const info = document.createElement('span');
    info.className = 'pagination-info';
    info.textContent = `Showing ${(page - 1) * perPage + 1}–${Math.min(page * perPage, total)} of ${total}`;
    container.appendChild(info);
  }

});
```

---

### 4. `rider/settings.php`

The rider's settings page is simpler than the customer's — no addresses section, no appeals section. Just profile management and password change.

**PHP Logic (top of file):**
```
1. Include auth_check.php, require_role([ROLE_RIDER])
2. Fetch current user data fresh from DB (not session cache):
   SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = session.user_id
3. Fetch user preferences:
   SELECT * FROM user_preferences WHERE user_id = session.user_id
4. Include header.php, sidebar.php
```

**HTML Structure:**
```html
<div class="main-content">
  <div class="page-header">
    <h1>Settings</h1>
    <p class="text-muted">Manage your profile and account settings.</p>
  </div>

  <!-- Profile Section -->
  <div class="settings-section glass-card">
    <h2><span class="material-icons">person</span> Profile Information</h2>
    <form id="profileForm">
      <div class="form-grid">
        <div class="float-input-group">
          <input type="text" id="profileUsername" class="float-input" value="<?= sanitize($user['username']) ?>" disabled
                 style="opacity: 0.6; cursor: not-allowed;">
          <label class="float-label">Username (cannot be changed)</label>
        </div>
        <div class="float-input-group">
          <input type="text" id="profileFullName" class="float-input" value="<?= sanitize($user['full_name']) ?>" placeholder=" " required>
          <label class="float-label">Full Name</label>
        </div>
        <div class="float-input-group">
          <input type="email" id="profileEmail" class="float-input" value="<?= sanitize($user['email']) ?>" placeholder=" " required>
          <label class="float-label">Email</label>
        </div>
        <div class="float-input-group">
          <input type="tel" id="profilePhone" class="float-input" value="<?= sanitize($user['phone']) ?>" placeholder=" " required>
          <label class="float-label">Phone Number</label>
        </div>
      </div>

      <!-- Account Info (read-only display) -->
      <div class="account-info">
        <div class="info-item">
          <span class="info-label">Role:</span>
          <span class="badge badge-rider">Rider</span>
        </div>
        <div class="info-item">
          <span class="info-label">Status:</span>
          <span class="badge badge-<?= $user['status'] ?>"><?= ucfirst($user['status']) ?></span>
        </div>
        <div class="info-item">
          <span class="info-label">Member since:</span>
          <span><?= format_date($user['created_at']) ?></span>
        </div>
      </div>

      <button type="submit" class="btn btn-primary">
        <span class="material-icons">save</span> Save Changes
      </button>
    </form>
  </div>

  <!-- Password Section -->
  <div class="settings-section glass-card">
    <h2><span class="material-icons">lock</span> Change Password</h2>
    <form id="passwordForm">
      <div class="form-grid">
        <div class="float-input-group">
          <input type="password" id="currentPassword" class="float-input" placeholder=" " required>
          <label class="float-label">Current Password</label>
        </div>
        <div class="float-input-group">
          <input type="password" id="newPassword" class="float-input" placeholder=" " required>
          <label class="float-label">New Password (min. 6 characters)</label>
        </div>
        <div class="float-input-group">
          <input type="password" id="confirmPassword" class="float-input" placeholder=" " required>
          <label class="float-label">Confirm New Password</label>
        </div>
      </div>
      <button type="submit" class="btn btn-warning">
        <span class="material-icons">lock_reset</span> Change Password
      </button>
    </form>
  </div>

  <!-- Availability Section -->
  <div class="settings-section glass-card">
    <h2><span class="material-icons">toggle_on</span> Availability</h2>
    <p class="text-muted" style="margin-bottom: 16px;">
      Control whether you receive new delivery assignments. You can also toggle this from your Dashboard.
    </p>
    <div class="availability-setting">
      <div class="availability-current">
        <span>Current status: </span>
        <strong id="settingsAvailStatus" class="<?= $user['is_available'] ? 'text-success' : 'text-danger' ?>">
          <?= $user['is_available'] ? 'Available' : 'Unavailable' ?>
        </strong>
      </div>
      <label class="toggle-switch">
        <input type="checkbox" id="settingsAvailToggle"
               <?= $user['is_available'] ? 'checked' : '' ?>
               <?php
                 // Check if rider has on_delivery orders — if so, disable toggle
                 $on_delivery_count = db_fetch("SELECT COUNT(*) as cnt FROM orders WHERE rider_id = ? AND status = 'on_delivery'", [$_SESSION['user_id']]);
                 if ($on_delivery_count && $on_delivery_count['cnt'] > 0) echo 'disabled title="Complete active deliveries first"';
               ?>>
        <span class="toggle-slider"></span>
      </label>
    </div>
    <?php if ($on_delivery_count && $on_delivery_count['cnt'] > 0): ?>
    <small class="text-warning" style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;margin-top:8px;">
      <span class="material-icons" style="font-size:16px;">warning</span>
      You have <?= $on_delivery_count['cnt'] ?> active delivery(ies). Complete them before going unavailable.
    </small>
    <?php endif; ?>
  </div>
</div>
```

### `rider/js/settings.js`

```javascript
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {

  // ===== PROFILE FORM =====
  document.getElementById('profileForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();

    const data = {
      full_name: document.getElementById('profileFullName').value.trim(),
      email: document.getElementById('profileEmail').value.trim(),
      phone: document.getElementById('profilePhone').value.trim()
    };

    if (!data.full_name || !data.email || !data.phone) {
      showToast('All fields are required', 'warning');
      return;
    }

    // Basic email validation
    if (!/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(data.email)) {
      showToast('Please enter a valid email address', 'warning');
      return;
    }

    const submitBtn = this.querySelector('button[type="submit"]');
    submitBtn.disabled = true;
    submitBtn.innerHTML = '<div class="spinner" style="width:18px;height:18px;"></div> Saving...';

    ajaxPost('/api/settings/update_profile.php', data)
      .then(res => {
        if (res.success) {
          showToast('Profile updated successfully', 'success');
        } else {
          showToast(res.message || 'Failed to update profile', 'error');
        }
      })
      .catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'))
      .finally(() => {
        submitBtn.disabled = false;
        submitBtn.innerHTML = '<span class="material-icons">save</span> Save Changes';
      });
  });

  // ===== PASSWORD FORM =====
  document.getElementById('passwordForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();

    const current = document.getElementById('currentPassword').value;
    const newPass = document.getElementById('newPassword').value;
    const confirm = document.getElementById('confirmPassword').value;

    if (!current || !newPass || !confirm) {
      showToast('All password fields are required', 'warning');
      return;
    }
    if (newPass.length < 6) {
      showToast('New password must be at least 6 characters', 'warning');
      return;
    }
    if (newPass !== confirm) {
      showToast('New passwords do not match', 'warning');
      return;
    }

    const submitBtn = this.querySelector('button[type="submit"]');
    submitBtn.disabled = true;
    submitBtn.innerHTML = '<div class="spinner" style="width:18px;height:18px;"></div> Changing...';

    ajaxPost('/api/settings/change_password.php', {
      current_password: current,
      new_password: newPass,
      confirm_password: confirm
    }).then(res => {
      if (res.success) {
        showToast('Password changed successfully', 'success');
        this.reset();
      } else {
        showToast(res.message || 'Failed to change password', 'error');
      }
    })
    .catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'))
    .finally(() => {
      submitBtn.disabled = false;
      submitBtn.innerHTML = '<span class="material-icons">lock_reset</span> Change Password';
    });
  });

  // ===== AVAILABILITY TOGGLE (in Settings) =====
  const settingsToggle = document.getElementById('settingsAvailToggle');
  if (settingsToggle && !settingsToggle.disabled) {
    settingsToggle.addEventListener('change', function() {
      const newState = this.checked;
      const confirmMsg = newState
        ? 'Set yourself as Available? You may receive new delivery assignments.'
        : 'Set yourself as Unavailable? You will not receive new delivery assignments.';

      Swal.fire({
        title: newState ? 'Go Available?' : 'Go Unavailable?',
        text: confirmMsg,
        icon: 'question',
        showCancelButton: true,
        confirmButtonText: newState ? 'Yes, Go Available' : 'Yes, Go Unavailable',
        cancelButtonText: 'Cancel',
        confirmButtonColor: newState ? 'var(--success)' : 'var(--warning)',
      }).then(result => {
        if (result.isConfirmed) {
          ajaxPost('/api/riders/toggle_availability.php', {})
            .then(data => {
              if (data.success) {
                showToast(
                  newState ? 'You are now available for deliveries' : 'You are now unavailable',
                  'success'
                );
                // Update the status text
                const statusText = document.getElementById('settingsAvailStatus');
                statusText.textContent = newState ? 'Available' : 'Unavailable';
                statusText.className = newState ? 'text-success' : 'text-danger';
              } else {
                settingsToggle.checked = !newState;
                showToast(data.message || 'Failed to update availability', 'error');
              }
            })
            .catch(() => {
              settingsToggle.checked = !newState;
              showToast('An error occurred', 'error');
            });
        } else {
          settingsToggle.checked = !newState;
        }
      });
    });
  }

});
```

## IMPORTANT IMPLEMENTATION NOTES FOR RIDER PAGES

1. **Rider accounts are always `status='active'`** from creation. There is no pending or flagged state for riders. No need to check for pending/flagged account status on rider pages (unlike customer pages). However, always verify the session role is `ROLE_RIDER` on every page.

2. **Riders ONLY see orders assigned to them.** The `api/orders/get_orders.php` endpoint scopes results by `rider_id = session.user_id` when the role is `rider`. The rider frontend should never display or attempt to access orders not assigned to them.

3. **Customer Details format in tables** must always be displayed as:
   ```
   Customer Full Name
   📞 Phone Number
   📍 Delivery Address (from the order's delivery_address field, or customer's default address)
   ```
   Use Material Icons (`phone`, `location_on`) inline before the phone and address. Each on its own line within the cell.

4. **Drag-and-drop priority reordering** uses Sortable.js attached to the `<tbody>` element. The `.drag-handle` class on the grip icon makes only that icon draggable (not the entire row). After each drag-and-drop, the new order is saved immediately to the server via `api/riders/update_priority.php`. Visual priority numbers are updated in real-time. The ghost/placeholder row during dragging should have reduced opacity and a subtle primary color background.

5. **Availability toggle appears in TWO places:** the Dashboard and the Settings page. Both use the same API endpoint (`api/riders/toggle_availability.php`). Both must show the confirmation SweetAlert before toggling. Both must handle the disabled/locked state when the rider has on_delivery orders. The toggle is a visual `<input type="checkbox">` styled as a toggle switch using the `.toggle-switch` and `.toggle-slider` CSS classes from `components.css`.

6. **When a rider cancels a delivery**, the order does NOT get status `cancelled`. Instead, it reverts to `confirmed` with `rider_id` set to NULL. This is a key distinction — the rider is just declining/returning the delivery, not cancelling the customer's order. Staff/Admin will then reassign to another rider. The cancellation reason from the rider is stored for Staff/Admin reference. The frontend dialog should say "Cancel Delivery" and explain "The order will be sent back to staff for reassignment."

7. **Performance stats on delivery_history.php** show:
   - Total Delivered: Count of orders with status `delivered` (or `accepted` or `picked_up`) WHERE `rider_id = this rider`
   - Total Cancelled: Count of orders that were reassigned away from this rider (this is tracked differently — the API should count based on session logs or a rider_cancelled flag. Alternatively, simplify: count orders in history where status = cancelled AND cancelled_by = rider's user_id)
   - Success Rate: `Completed / (Completed + Cancelled) × 100`%
   - The `api/riders/get_statistics.php` with `self=true` parameter returns these stats for the logged-in rider.

8. **Item icons** in tables: same as customer — if item has `item_icon`, show that image. If NULL, show `/assets/images/default-item.png`. Use `.item-icon-sm` class (20-24px, rounded corners).

9. **Every AJAX call** must use `ajaxPost()` or `ajaxGet()` from `global.js` which automatically attach the CSRF token. Every call must have `.catch()` error handling that shows a toast.

10. **All dates** must be formatted in Philippine timezone. Use the JS `formatDate()` function which renders dates as "Jun 30, 2025 02:30 PM".

11. **Each page-specific JS file** must be wrapped in `document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() { ... })`.

12. **Dark mode support** is handled entirely via CSS variables. All page-specific CSS should ONLY use CSS custom properties for colors — never hardcode colors. This ensures dark mode works automatically when `data-theme="dark"` is set on `<html>`.

13. **The rider has NO access to:** placing orders, viewing inventory, managing accounts, viewing analytics, session logs, or system settings. The sidebar only shows: Dashboard, Assigned Deliveries, Delivery History, Settings. If a rider tries to access any other page, the `require_role([ROLE_RIDER])` check and proper URL routing should prevent it.

14. **Tables render max 50 items per page** with pagination showing Previous/Next buttons and "Showing X-Y of Z items" counter.

15. **Glass card effect** is used for: stat cards, settings sections, availability toggle card on dashboard. Not overused — keep it subtle and professional.

16. **Bulk actions bar** appears only when one or more checkboxes are checked. It slides down with animation. When no items are checked, it hides. The "Select All" checkbox in the table header toggles all visible checkboxes. Bulk actions respect the same rules as individual actions — e.g., bulk "Mark Delivered" only applies to `on_delivery` orders, bulk "Mark On Delivery" only applies to `assigned` orders. If a mixed selection is made, the API processes valid ones and reports how many succeeded vs failed.

---

Every CSS file must include all styles described including responsive breakpoints and dark mode support via CSS variables. Every JS file must include all interactivity, AJAX calls, SweetAlert2 dialogs, Sortable.js integration, and error handling as described. Do not use placeholders or TODO comments.**

# PROMPT #4 — STAFF ROLE (All Pages, CSS, JS)

You are continuing the build of **"Azeu Water Station"** — a Philippine-based Water Refilling Station management web application. In previous prompts, the entire foundation was built: config files (`database.php`, `session.php`, `constants.php`, `functions.php`, `AESCrypt.php`, `logger.php`), all shared assets (`global.css`, `auth.css`, `components.css`, `layout.css`, `receipt.css`, `global.js`, `auth.js`, `components.js`, `sidebar.js`, `receipt.js`), all includes (`header.php`, `sidebar.php`, `footer.php`, `auth_check.php`), ALL API endpoints (`api/` folder — auth, orders, accounts, inventory, riders, addresses, appeals, notifications, settings, analytics), public pages (`index.php`, `register.php`, `forgot_password.php`, `reset_password.php`, `receipt.php`, `maintenance.php`), error pages, logging system, the complete customer role (`customer/` folder — 5 pages + CSS + JS), and the complete rider role (`rider/` folder — 4 pages + CSS + JS).

## PROJECT CONTEXT RECAP

Azeu Water Station is a web-based order and delivery management system for a water refilling station in the Philippines. It has 4 roles: Customer, Rider, Staff, Admin (with Super Admin). The tech stack is pure PHP (no frameworks), MySQL on XAMPP (database name: `station_azeu`), and hand-written HTML/CSS/JS. No frameworks, no Bootstrap, no Tailwind.

**Staff** are operational managers who:
- Cannot register themselves — accounts are created by Admin/Super Admin only
- Are always `status='active'` from creation (skip pending approval)
- Approve or delete pending customer accounts after registration
- Create Customer and Rider accounts (NOT Staff or Admin — only Admin can create Staff)
- Edit and delete (soft-delete) Customer and Rider accounts
- Confirm customer orders (which triggers stock decrement from inventory)
- Assign riders to confirmed orders (manually select or auto-assign least-loaded available rider)
- Reassign riders on assigned orders
- Update order status at any stage (Pending, Confirmed, Assigned, On Delivery, Delivered, Ready for Pickup, Picked Up)
- Cancel orders at any status with a mandatory reason
- Add staff comments to orders (visible to customers, e.g., "Waiting for available rider")
- Mark pickup orders as "Ready for Pickup" and "Picked Up"
- View inventory in read-only mode (see stock counts, prices, statuses — cannot add/edit/remove items)
- View rider performance statistics (completed deliveries, success rates, current loads)
- Review and approve/deny customer cancellation appeals
- View all order history with filters and search
- Manage their own profile and password
- Perform bulk actions on orders (bulk confirm, bulk cancel, bulk assign)

**Staff CANNOT:**
- Create Staff, Admin, or Super Admin accounts (only Admin+ can do this)
- See Staff, Admin, or Super Admin accounts in Account Management (only Customer and Rider accounts visible)
- Modify inventory (read-only access)
- Access Analytics, Session Logs, or System Settings pages (Admin-only features)
- Modify or delete the Super Admin account

## ORDER LIFECYCLE (Staff Perspective — Full Control)

Staff has the highest operational authority over orders (same level as Admin for order management). Staff can perform all status transitions except they cannot modify system settings.

### Delivery Orders (Cash on Delivery) — Full Flow
```
PENDING ──► CONFIRMED ──► ASSIGNED ──► ON DELIVERY ──► DELIVERED ──► ACCEPTED (by customer)
   │             │             │              │               │
   │             │             │              │               └── Final (no staff action)
   │             │             │              └── Staff can: Update status, Cancel
   │             │             └── Staff can: Reassign rider, Cancel
   │             └── Staff can: Assign rider, Cancel, Mark Ready for Pickup (if pickup type)
   └── Staff can: Confirm (triggers stock decrement), Cancel
```

### Pickup Orders — Full Flow
```
PENDING ──► CONFIRMED ──► READY FOR PICKUP ──► PICKED UP ──► ACCEPTED (by customer)
   │             │                │                 │
   │             │                │                 └── Final
   │             │                └── Staff can: Mark Picked Up, Cancel
   │             └── Staff can: Mark Ready for Pickup, Cancel
   └── Staff can: Confirm, Cancel
```

### Staff Order Actions by Status

| Current Status | Available Actions | Details |
|----------------|-------------------|---------|
| **Pending** | Confirm, Cancel | Confirm: decrements stock, creates notification. Optionally assign rider immediately ("Assign now?" dialog). Cancel: reason required, stock NOT restored (never decremented). |
| **Confirmed** (no rider) | Assign Rider, Ready for Pickup (pickup only), Cancel | Assign: Select rider manually or Auto-assign. Cancel: reason required, stock IS restored. |
| **Confirmed** (pickup, no rider) | Ready for Pickup, Cancel | Move to Ready for Pickup. |
| **Assigned** (has rider) | Reassign Rider, Cancel | Reassign: select different rider. Cancel: reason required, stock IS restored, rider notified. |
| **On Delivery** | Update Status, Cancel | Update: change to Pending/Confirmed/Delivered/any status. Cancel: reason required, stock IS restored, rider notified. |
| **Ready for Pickup** | Picked Up, Cancel | Mark Picked Up: income counted. Cancel: stock restored. |
| **Delivered** | (View only) | Cannot change. Income already counted. |
| **Picked Up** | (View only) | Cannot change. Income already counted. |
| **Accepted** | (View only) | Customer confirmed receipt. |
| **Cancelled** | (View only in history) | Final state. |

### Stock Management Rules (Staff Must Understand)
- **Stock decremented** when order moves from `Pending` → `Confirmed`
- **Stock restored** when any order that was `Confirmed` or beyond is `Cancelled`
- **Stock NOT restored** when a `Pending` order is cancelled (stock was never decremented)
- Staff can see current stock levels in the read-only Inventory page to make informed decisions

### Auto-Assign Rider Algorithm
When staff clicks "Auto" assign:
1. Get all riders WHERE `role='rider'` AND `status='active'` AND `is_available=1` AND `deleted_at IS NULL`
2. For each rider, COUNT their current orders WHERE status IN `('assigned','on_delivery')` → this is "current_load"
3. Sort by `current_load ASC` (least loaded first)
4. If tied, sort by `rider.id ASC` (first registered)
5. If NO available riders → return failure, order stays Confirmed, staff can optionally add a comment like "Waiting for available rider" visible to the customer
6. If rider found → assign, set status to `assigned`, create `delivery_priority` entry, notify rider + customer

### Order Grouping in Manage Orders
Orders from the **same customer** with the **same status** should be visually grouped in the table:
- They appear as one expandable/collapsible row showing the customer name, total items count across all orders, and combined status
- Clicking the row expands to show individual orders underneath
- Bulk actions on the grouped row apply to ALL orders in that group
- This makes it easier for staff to manage multiple orders from one customer

---

## STAFF SIDEBAR NAVIGATION

```
Dashboard              → staff/dashboard.php              icon: dashboard
Account Management     → staff/account_management.php     icon: people
Manage Orders          → staff/manage_orders.php          icon: list_alt
Order History          → staff/order_history.php          icon: history
Inventory              → staff/inventory.php              icon: inventory_2
Rider Statistics       → staff/rider_statistics.php       icon: bar_chart
Settings               → staff/settings.php               icon: settings
```

---

## PAGE-BY-PAGE SPECIFICATIONS

---

### 1. `staff/dashboard.php`

**PHP Logic (top of file):**
```
1. Include auth_check.php, require_role([ROLE_STAFF])
2. Fetch dashboard stats:
   - Pending orders count: SELECT COUNT(*) FROM orders WHERE status='pending'
   - Confirmed orders count: SELECT COUNT(*) FROM orders WHERE status='confirmed'
   - On delivery orders count: SELECT COUNT(*) FROM orders WHERE status='on_delivery'
   - Pending accounts count: SELECT COUNT(*) FROM users WHERE status='pending'
   - Total riders count: SELECT COUNT(*) FROM users WHERE role='rider' AND status='active' AND deleted_at IS NULL
   - Available riders count: SELECT COUNT(*) FROM users WHERE role='rider' AND status='active' AND is_available=1 AND deleted_at IS NULL
3. Fetch pending accounts preview (max 3, newest first):
   SELECT * FROM users WHERE status='pending'
   AND role IN ('customer','rider')
   ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT 3
4. Fetch pending orders preview (max 3, newest first):
   SELECT o.*, u.full_name as customer_name, u.phone as customer_phone,
   GROUP_CONCAT(oi.item_name) as item_names
   FROM orders o
   LEFT JOIN users u ON o.customer_id = u.id
   LEFT JOIN order_items oi ON o.id = oi.order_id
   WHERE o.status = 'pending'
   GROUP BY o.id
   ORDER BY o.created_at DESC LIMIT 3
5. Include header.php, sidebar.php
```

**HTML Structure:**
```html
<div class="main-content">
  <div class="page-header">
    <h1>Dashboard</h1>
  </div>

  <!-- Greeting -->
  <div class="greeting">
    <h2>Welcome back, {Full Name}! 👋</h2>
    <p class="text-muted">Here's an overview of station operations.</p>
  </div>

  <!-- Quick Action Buttons -->
  <div class="quick-actions">
    <a href="account_management.php" class="quick-action-btn">
      <span class="material-icons">people</span>
      <span>Accounts</span>
    </a>
    <a href="manage_orders.php" class="quick-action-btn">
      <span class="material-icons">list_alt</span>
      <span>Manage Orders</span>
    </a>
    <a href="order_history.php" class="quick-action-btn">
      <span class="material-icons">history</span>
      <span>Order History</span>
    </a>
    <a href="inventory.php" class="quick-action-btn">
      <span class="material-icons">inventory_2</span>
      <span>Inventory</span>
    </a>
    <a href="rider_statistics.php" class="quick-action-btn">
      <span class="material-icons">bar_chart</span>
      <span>Rider Stats</span>
    </a>
    <a href="settings.php" class="quick-action-btn">
      <span class="material-icons">settings</span>
      <span>Settings</span>
    </a>
  </div>

  <!-- Stat Cards - 2 rows of 3 -->
  <div class="stats-grid">
    <div class="stat-card">
      <div class="stat-icon" style="background: var(--warning)">
        <span class="material-icons">pending_actions</span>
      </div>
      <div class="stat-info">
        <span class="stat-number">{pending_orders}</span>
        <span class="stat-label">Pending Orders</span>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="stat-card">
      <div class="stat-icon" style="background: var(--info)">
        <span class="material-icons">check_circle_outline</span>
      </div>
```
