```html
        <span class="stat-number">{confirmed_orders}</span>
        <span class="stat-label">Confirmed Orders</span>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="stat-card">
      <div class="stat-icon" style="background: var(--teal)">
        <span class="material-icons">local_shipping</span>
      </div>
      <div class="stat-info">
        <span class="stat-number">{on_delivery_orders}</span>
        <span class="stat-label">On Delivery</span>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="stat-card">
      <div class="stat-icon" style="background: var(--danger)">
        <span class="material-icons">person_add</span>
      </div>
      <div class="stat-info">
        <span class="stat-number">{pending_accounts}</span>
        <span class="stat-label">Pending Accounts</span>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="stat-card">
      <div class="stat-icon" style="background: var(--purple)">
        <span class="material-icons">delivery_dining</span>
      </div>
      <div class="stat-info">
        <span class="stat-number">{total_riders}</span>
        <span class="stat-label">Total Riders</span>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="stat-card">
      <div class="stat-icon" style="background: var(--success)">
        <span class="material-icons">how_to_reg</span>
      </div>
      <div class="stat-info">
        <span class="stat-number">{available_riders}</span>
        <span class="stat-label">Available Riders</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

  <!-- Two-column preview section -->
  <div class="preview-grid">
    <!-- Pending Accounts Preview -->
    <div class="preview-section glass-card">
      <div class="preview-header">
        <h3><span class="material-icons">person_add</span> Pending Accounts</h3>
        <a href="account_management.php" class="btn btn-outline btn-sm">View All</a>
      </div>
      <!-- IF NO PENDING ACCOUNTS -->
      <div class="empty-state mini" style="display: {if none}">
        <span class="material-icons">check_circle</span>
        <p>No pending accounts</p>
      </div>
      <!-- IF PENDING ACCOUNTS EXIST -->
      <div class="data-table-wrapper" style="display: {if exist}">
        <table class="data-table compact">
          <thead>
            <tr>
              <th>Username</th>
              <th>Full Name</th>
              <th>Role</th>
              <th>Registered</th>
              <th>Actions</th>
            </tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody>
            <!-- For each pending account (max 3): -->
            <tr>
              <td>{username}</td>
              <td>{full_name}</td>
              <td><span class="badge {role_badge_class}">{role}</span></td>
              <td>{time_ago(created_at)}</td>
              <td>
                <button class="btn-icon btn-success" title="Approve"
                        onclick="quickApprove({user_id}, '{username}')">
                  <span class="material-icons">check</span>
                </button>
                <button class="btn-icon btn-danger" title="Delete"
                        onclick="quickDelete({user_id}, '{username}')">
                  <span class="material-icons">delete</span>
                </button>
              </td>
            </tr>
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- Pending Orders Preview -->
    <div class="preview-section glass-card">
      <div class="preview-header">
        <h3><span class="material-icons">pending_actions</span> Pending Orders</h3>
        <a href="manage_orders.php" class="btn btn-outline btn-sm">View All</a>
      </div>
      <!-- IF NO PENDING ORDERS -->
      <div class="empty-state mini" style="display: {if none}">
        <span class="material-icons">check_circle</span>
        <p>No pending orders</p>
      </div>
      <!-- IF PENDING ORDERS EXIST -->
      <div class="data-table-wrapper" style="display: {if exist}">
        <table class="data-table compact">
          <thead>
            <tr>
              <th>Order ID</th>
              <th>Customer</th>
              <th>Items</th>
              <th>Payment</th>
              <th>Ordered</th>
              <th>Actions</th>
            </tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody>
            <!-- For each pending order (max 3): -->
            <tr>
              <td><strong>#{order_id}</strong></td>
              <td>{customer_name}</td>
              <td>{item_names (truncated)}</td>
              <td>{payment_type label}</td>
              <td>{time_ago(order_date)}</td>
              <td>
                <button class="btn-icon btn-success" title="Confirm"
                        onclick="quickConfirm({order_id})">
                  <span class="material-icons">check_circle</span>
                </button>
                <button class="btn-icon btn-danger" title="Cancel"
                        onclick="quickCancelOrder({order_id})">
                  <span class="material-icons">cancel</span>
                </button>
              </td>
            </tr>
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>
```

### `staff/css/dashboard.css`

```
.greeting:
  - margin-bottom 20px
  - h2: font-weight 600

.stats-grid:
  - CSS Grid: 3 columns desktop, 2 tablet, 1 mobile
  - Gap: 16px
  - Margin-bottom: 24px

.stat-card:
  - Glass card, flex row, align center, gap 16px, padding 20px
  - .stat-icon: 48x48px circle, flex center, border-radius 50%, color white
  - .stat-number: font-size 1.8em, font-weight 700
  - .stat-label: font-size 0.85em, color var(--text-muted)

.preview-grid:
  - CSS Grid: 2 columns on desktop (equal width), 1 column on mobile
  - Gap: 20px

.preview-section:
  - Padding: 20px
  - .preview-header: flex row, space-between, align center, margin-bottom 16px
    h3: flex row, align center, gap 8px, font-size 1.1em

.data-table.compact:
  - Smaller padding on cells (8px 12px)
  - Font-size: 0.9em

.empty-state.mini:
  - Padding: 24px (smaller than full empty state)
  - Icon: font-size 36px

Responsive:
  @media (max-width: 1024px):
    - preview-grid: 1 column
  @media (max-width: 768px):
    - stats-grid: 1 column
    - quick-actions: flex wrap
```

### `staff/js/dashboard.js`

```javascript
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {

  // Quick Approve Account from dashboard preview
  window.quickApprove = function(userId, username) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Approve Account?',
      text: `Are you sure you want to approve "${username}"?`,
      icon: 'question',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Yes, Approve',
      cancelButtonText: 'No',
      confirmButtonColor: 'var(--success)'
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/accounts/approve.php', { user_id: userId })
          .then(data => {
            if (data.success) {
              showToast(`Account "${username}" approved!`, 'success');
              location.reload();
            } else {
              showToast(data.message || 'Failed to approve', 'error');
            }
          }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  };

  // Quick Delete Pending Account from dashboard
  window.quickDelete = function(userId, username) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Delete Account?',
      text: `Are you sure you want to delete "${username}"? This action cannot be undone.`,
      icon: 'warning',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Yes, Delete',
      cancelButtonText: 'No',
      confirmButtonColor: '#EF5350'
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/accounts/delete.php', { user_id: userId })
          .then(data => {
            if (data.success) {
              showToast(`Account "${username}" deleted`, 'success');
              location.reload();
            } else {
              showToast(data.message || 'Failed to delete', 'error');
            }
          }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  };

  // Quick Confirm Order from dashboard
  window.quickConfirm = function(orderId) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Confirm Order?',
      html: `
        <p>Confirm Order <strong>#${orderId}</strong>?</p>
        <p style="color:var(--text-muted);font-size:0.9em;margin-top:8px;">
          Stock will be decremented for all items in this order.
        </p>
      `,
      icon: 'question',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Confirm Order',
      cancelButtonText: 'Cancel',
      confirmButtonColor: 'var(--success)'
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/orders/update_status.php', {
          order_id: orderId,
          new_status: 'confirmed'
        }).then(data => {
          if (data.success) {
            // Ask about rider assignment
            Swal.fire({
              title: 'Order Confirmed!',
              text: 'Do you want to assign a rider to this order now?',
              icon: 'success',
              showCancelButton: true,
              confirmButtonText: 'Yes, Assign Now',
              cancelButtonText: 'Later',
              confirmButtonColor: 'var(--primary)'
            }).then(assignResult => {
              if (assignResult.isConfirmed) {
                window.location.href = 'manage_orders.php?highlight=' + orderId;
              } else {
                location.reload();
              }
            });
          } else {
            showToast(data.message || 'Failed to confirm', 'error');
          }
        }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  };

  // Quick Cancel Order from dashboard
  window.quickCancelOrder = function(orderId) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Cancel Order #' + orderId + '?',
      html: `<textarea id="cancelReason" class="swal2-textarea"
              placeholder="Reason for cancellation (required)" rows="3"></textarea>`,
      icon: 'warning',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Yes, Cancel Order',
      cancelButtonText: 'No, Keep It',
      confirmButtonColor: '#EF5350',
      preConfirm: () => {
        const reason = document.getElementById('cancelReason').value.trim();
        if (!reason) {
          Swal.showValidationMessage('Please provide a cancellation reason');
          return false;
        }
        return reason;
      }
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/orders/cancel_order.php', {
          order_id: orderId,
          reason: result.value
        }).then(data => {
          if (data.success) {
            showToast('Order cancelled', 'success');
            location.reload();
          } else {
            showToast(data.message || 'Failed to cancel', 'error');
          }
        }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  };

});
```

---

### 2. `staff/account_management.php`

**PHP Logic:**
```
1. Include auth_check.php, require_role([ROLE_STAFF])
2. Data loaded via AJAX
3. Include header.php, sidebar.php
```

**HTML Structure:**
```html
<div class="main-content">
  <div class="page-header">
    <div class="page-header-left">
      <h1>Account Management</h1>
      <p class="text-muted">Manage customer and rider accounts.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="page-header-right">
      <button class="btn btn-primary" id="addAccountBtn">
        <span class="material-icons">person_add</span> Add Account
      </button>
    </div>
  </div>

  <!-- Toolbar: Filters + Search -->
  <div class="toolbar">
    <div class="filter-bar" id="accountFilters">
      <button class="filter-btn active" data-filter="all">All</button>
      <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="pending">Pending</button>
      <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="active">Active</button>
      <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="flagged">Flagged</button>
      <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="customer">Customers</button>
      <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="rider">Riders</button>
    </div>
    <div class="search-bar">
      <span class="material-icons search-icon">search</span>
      <input type="text" id="accountSearch" class="search-input" placeholder="Search username, name, email...">
    </div>
  </div>

  <!-- Accounts Table -->
  <div class="data-table-wrapper">
    <table class="data-table" id="accountsTable">
      <thead>
        <tr>
          <th>Role</th>
          <th>Account ID</th>
          <th>Username</th>
          <th>Full Name</th>
          <th>Email</th>
          <th>Address</th>
          <th>Phone</th>
          <th>Status</th>
          <th>Created</th>
          <th>Actions</th>
        </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody id="accountsBody">
        <tr class="loading-row"><td colspan="10"><div class="spinner"></div></td></tr>
      </tbody>
    </table>
  </div>

  <div class="pagination" id="accountsPagination"></div>

  <div class="empty-state" id="emptyAccounts" style="display:none;">
    <span class="material-icons">people</span>
    <p>No accounts found.</p>
  </div>

  <!-- Cancellation Appeals Section -->
  <div class="appeals-section glass-card" id="appealsSection">
    <div class="preview-header">
      <h3><span class="material-icons">gavel</span> Cancellation Appeals</h3>
    </div>
    <div class="data-table-wrapper">
      <table class="data-table" id="appealsTable">
        <thead>
          <tr>
            <th>Customer</th>
            <th>Reason</th>
            <th>Submitted</th>
            <th>Status</th>
            <th>Actions</th>
          </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody id="appealsBody">
          <tr class="loading-row"><td colspan="5"><div class="spinner"></div></td></tr>
        </tbody>
      </table>
    </div>
    <div class="empty-state mini" id="emptyAppeals" style="display:none;">
      <span class="material-icons">check_circle</span>
      <p>No pending appeals</p>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>
```

### `staff/css/account_management.css`

```
.page-header:
  - Flex row, space-between, align center, flex wrap
  - Gap: 16px

.toolbar:
  - Flex row, space-between, align center, flex wrap
  - Gap: 12px
  - Margin-bottom: 16px

.filter-bar:
  - Overflow-x auto on mobile
  - Gap 6px

.data-table:
  - Pending accounts should have a subtle highlighted row background:
    tr.pending-row { background: rgba(255, 167, 38, 0.05); border-left: 3px solid var(--warning); }
  - td with addresses: max-width 200px, truncated, title tooltip
  - Status badges: colored per status

.appeals-section:
  - Margin-top: 32px
  - Padding: 20px
  - Border-top: 2px solid var(--border)

Responsive:
  @media (max-width: 768px):
    - page-header: flex column, align start
    - toolbar: flex column
    - Add Account button: full width
    - Table horizontal scroll
```

### `staff/js/account_management.js`

```javascript
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {

  let currentFilter = 'all';
  let currentPage = 1;
  let searchText = '';
  const perPage = 50;

  loadAccounts();
  loadAppeals();

  // ===== FILTER BUTTONS =====
  document.querySelectorAll('#accountFilters .filter-btn').forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      document.querySelectorAll('#accountFilters .filter-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
      this.classList.add('active');
      currentFilter = this.dataset.filter;
      currentPage = 1;
      loadAccounts();
    });
  });

  // ===== SEARCH =====
  let searchTimeout;
  document.getElementById('accountSearch').addEventListener('input', function() {
    clearTimeout(searchTimeout);
    searchTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
      searchText = this.value.trim();
      currentPage = 1;
      loadAccounts();
    }, 300);
  });

  // ===== LOAD ACCOUNTS =====
  function loadAccounts() {
    let filterRole = '';
    let filterStatus = '';

    if (['customer', 'rider'].includes(currentFilter)) {
      filterRole = currentFilter;
    } else if (['pending', 'active', 'flagged'].includes(currentFilter)) {
      filterStatus = currentFilter;
    }

    const params = {
      filter_role: filterRole,
      filter_status: filterStatus,
      search: searchText,
      page: currentPage
    };

    document.getElementById('accountsBody').innerHTML =
      '<tr class="loading-row"><td colspan="10"><div class="spinner"></div></td></tr>';
    document.getElementById('emptyAccounts').style.display = 'none';

    ajaxGet('/api/accounts/get_accounts.php', params)
      .then(data => {
        if (!data.accounts || data.accounts.length === 0) {
          document.getElementById('accountsBody').innerHTML = '';
          document.getElementById('emptyAccounts').style.display = 'flex';
          document.getElementById('accountsPagination').innerHTML = '';
          return;
        }
        document.getElementById('emptyAccounts').style.display = 'none';
        renderAccounts(data.accounts);
        renderPagination(data.total, data.page, data.per_page, 'accountsPagination', loadAccounts);
      })
      .catch(() => showToast('Failed to load accounts', 'error'));
  }

  // ===== RENDER ACCOUNTS =====
  function renderAccounts(accounts) {
    const tbody = document.getElementById('accountsBody');
    tbody.innerHTML = '';

    accounts.forEach(acc => {
      const tr = document.createElement('tr');
      if (acc.status === 'pending') tr.classList.add('pending-row');

      const isPending = acc.status === 'pending';
      const roleLabel = acc.role.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + acc.role.slice(1);

      let actionsHtml = '';
      if (isPending) {
        actionsHtml = `
          <button class="btn-icon btn-success" title="Approve" onclick="approveAccount(${acc.id}, '${escapeHtml(acc.username)}')">
            <span class="material-icons">check</span>
          </button>
          <button class="btn-icon btn-danger" title="Delete" onclick="deleteAccount(${acc.id}, '${escapeHtml(acc.username)}')">
            <span class="material-icons">delete</span>
          </button>
        `;
      } else {
        actionsHtml = `
          <button class="btn-icon btn-info" title="Edit" onclick="editAccount(${acc.id})">
            <span class="material-icons">edit</span>
          </button>
          <button class="btn-icon btn-danger" title="Delete" onclick="deleteAccount(${acc.id}, '${escapeHtml(acc.username)}')">
            <span class="material-icons">delete</span>
          </button>
        `;
      }

      // Get default address for display
      const addressDisplay = acc.default_address || '<span class="text-muted">—</span>';

      tr.innerHTML = `
        <td><span class="badge badge-${acc.role}">${roleLabel}</span></td>
        <td>${acc.id}</td>
        <td><strong>${escapeHtml(acc.username)}</strong></td>
        <td>${escapeHtml(acc.full_name)}</td>
        <td>${escapeHtml(acc.email)}</td>
        <td class="truncate-cell" title="${escapeHtml(acc.default_address || '')}">${addressDisplay}</td>
        <td>${escapeHtml(acc.phone)}</td>
        <td><span class="badge badge-${acc.status}">${acc.status.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + acc.status.slice(1)}</span></td>
        <td>${formatDate(acc.created_at)}</td>
        <td class="actions-cell">${actionsHtml}</td>
      `;

      tbody.appendChild(tr);
    });
  }

  // ===== ADD ACCOUNT =====
  document.getElementById('addAccountBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Add New Account',
      html: `
        <div style="text-align:left;">
          <div style="margin-bottom:12px;">
            <label style="font-weight:500;margin-bottom:4px;display:block;color:var(--text-secondary);">Role</label>
            <select id="newRole" class="swal2-select" style="width:100%;">
              <option value="customer">Customer</option>
              <option value="rider">Rider</option>
            </select>
          </div>
          <input type="text" id="newFullName" class="swal2-input" placeholder="Full Name">
          <input type="text" id="newUsername" class="swal2-input" placeholder="Username">
          <input type="email" id="newEmail" class="swal2-input" placeholder="Email">
          <input type="tel" id="newPhone" class="swal2-input" placeholder="Phone Number">
          <input type="password" id="newPassword" class="swal2-input" placeholder="Password">
          <div id="addressField">
            <input type="text" id="newAddress" class="swal2-input" placeholder="Full Address (for customers)">
          </div>
        </div>
      `,
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Create Account',
      cancelButtonText: 'Cancel',
      confirmButtonColor: 'var(--primary)',
      didOpen: () => {
        // Show/hide address field based on role
        document.getElementById('newRole').addEventListener('change', function() {
          document.getElementById('addressField').style.display =
            this.value === 'customer' ? 'block' : 'none';
        });
      },
      preConfirm: () => {
        const role = document.getElementById('newRole').value;
        const fullName = document.getElementById('newFullName').value.trim();
        const username = document.getElementById('newUsername').value.trim();
        const email = document.getElementById('newEmail').value.trim();
        const phone = document.getElementById('newPhone').value.trim();
        const password = document.getElementById('newPassword').value;
        const address = document.getElementById('newAddress').value.trim();

        if (!fullName || !username || !email || !phone || !password) {
          Swal.showValidationMessage('All fields except address are required');
          return false;
        }
        if (role === 'customer' && !address) {
          Swal.showValidationMessage('Address is required for customers');
          return false;
        }
        if (password.length < 6) {
          Swal.showValidationMessage('Password must be at least 6 characters');
          return false;
        }

        return { role, full_name: fullName, username, email, phone, password, full_address: address };
      }
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/accounts/create.php', result.value)
          .then(data => {
            if (data.success) {
              showToast('Account created successfully', 'success');
              loadAccounts();
            } else {
              showToast(data.message || 'Failed to create account', 'error');
            }
          }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  });

  // ===== APPROVE ACCOUNT =====
  window.approveAccount = function(userId, username) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Approve Account?',
      text: `Are you sure you want to approve "${username}"?`,
      icon: 'question',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Yes, Approve',
      cancelButtonText: 'No',
      confirmButtonColor: 'var(--success)'
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/accounts/approve.php', { user_id: userId })
          .then(data => {
            if (data.success) {
              showToast(`"${username}" approved!`, 'success');
              loadAccounts();
            } else {
              showToast(data.message || 'Failed to approve', 'error');
            }
          }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  };

  // ===== EDIT ACCOUNT =====
  window.editAccount = function(userId) {
    // Fetch current account data first
    ajaxGet('/api/accounts/get_accounts.php', { user_id: userId })
      .then(data => {
        const acc = data.account || data.accounts?.find(a => a.id === userId);
        if (!acc) { showToast('Account not found', 'error'); return; }

        Swal.fire({
          title: 'Edit Account',
          html: `
            <div style="text-align:left;">
              <p style="margin-bottom:12px;color:var(--text-muted);">Username: <strong>${escapeHtml(acc.username)}</strong> (cannot be changed)</p>
              <input type="text" id="editFullName" class="swal2-input" placeholder="Full Name" value="${escapeHtml(acc.full_name)}">
              <input type="email" id="editEmail" class="swal2-input" placeholder="Email" value="${escapeHtml(acc.email)}">
              <input type="tel" id="editPhone" class="swal2-input" placeholder="Phone" value="${escapeHtml(acc.phone)}">
              <input type="password" id="editPassword" class="swal2-input" placeholder="New Password (leave blank to keep current)">
            </div>
          `,
          showCancelButton: true,
          confirmButtonText: 'Save Changes',
          cancelButtonText: 'Cancel',
          confirmButtonColor: 'var(--primary)',
          preConfirm: () => {
            const fullName = document.getElementById('editFullName').value.trim();
            const email = document.getElementById('editEmail').value.trim();
            const phone = document.getElementById('editPhone').value.trim();
            const password = document.getElementById('editPassword').value;

            if (!fullName || !email || !phone) {
              Swal.showValidationMessage('Name, email, and phone are required');
              return false;
            }
            if (password && password.length < 6) {
              Swal.showValidationMessage('Password must be at least 6 characters');
              return false;
            }

            const payload = { user_id: userId, full_name: fullName, email, phone };
            if (password) payload.password = password;
            return payload;
          }
        }).then(result => {
          if (result.isConfirmed) {
            ajaxPost('/api/accounts/update.php', result.value)
              .then(data => {
                if (data.success) {
                  showToast('Account updated', 'success');
                  loadAccounts();
                } else {
                  showToast(data.message || 'Failed to update', 'error');
                }
              }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
          }
        });
      }).catch(() => showToast('Failed to load account data', 'error'));
  };

  // ===== DELETE ACCOUNT =====
  window.deleteAccount = function(userId, username) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Delete Account?',
      text: `Are you sure you want to delete "${username}"? This cannot be undone for pending accounts. Active accounts with orders will be soft-deleted.`,
      icon: 'warning',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Yes, Delete',
      cancelButtonText: 'No',
      confirmButtonColor: '#EF5350'
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/accounts/delete.php', { user_id: userId })
          .then(data => {
            if (data.success) {
              showToast(`"${username}" deleted`, 'success');
              loadAccounts();
            } else {
              showToast(data.message || 'Failed to delete', 'error');
            }
          }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  };

  // ===== LOAD APPEALS =====
  function loadAppeals() {
    ajaxGet('/api/appeals/get.php', { status_filter: 'pending' })
      .then(data => {
        if (!data.appeals || data.appeals.length === 0) {
          document.getElementById('appealsBody').innerHTML = '';
          document.getElementById('emptyAppeals').style.display = 'flex';
          return;
        }
        document.getElementById('emptyAppeals').style.display = 'none';
        renderAppeals(data.appeals);
      })
      .catch(() => {});
  }

  function renderAppeals(appeals) {
    const tbody = document.getElementById('appealsBody');
    tbody.innerHTML = '';

    appeals.forEach(appeal => {
      const tr = document.createElement('tr');
      tr.innerHTML = `
        <td><strong>${escapeHtml(appeal.customer_name || 'Unknown')}</strong><br>
          <small class="text-muted">${escapeHtml(appeal.customer_username || '')}</small></td>
        <td class="truncate-cell" title="${escapeHtml(appeal.reason)}">${escapeHtml(appeal.reason)}</td>
        <td>${formatDate(appeal.created_at)}</td>
        <td><span class="badge badge-${appeal.status}">${appeal.status.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + appeal.status.slice(1)}</span></td>
        <td class="actions-cell">
          <button class="btn-icon btn-success" title="Approve Appeal" onclick="reviewAppeal(${appeal.id}, 'approved')">
            <span class="material-icons">check</span>
          </button>
          <button class="btn-icon btn-danger" title="Deny Appeal" onclick="reviewAppeal(${appeal.id}, 'denied')">
            <span class="material-icons">close</span>
          </button>
        </td>
      `;
      tbody.appendChild(tr);
    });
  }

  // ===== REVIEW APPEAL =====
  window.reviewAppeal = function(appealId, decision) {
    const title = decision === 'approved' ? 'Approve Appeal?' : 'Deny Appeal?';
    const desc = decision === 'approved'
      ? 'The customer\'s account will be unflagged and cancellation count reset to 0.'
      : 'The customer will remain flagged.';

    Swal.fire({
      title: title,
      html: `
        <p>${desc}</p>
        <textarea id="appealNotes" class="swal2-textarea"
          placeholder="Admin notes (optional)" rows="3"></textarea>
      `,
      icon: decision === 'approved' ? 'question' : 'warning',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: decision === 'approved' ? 'Approve' : 'Deny',
      confirmButtonColor: decision === 'approved' ? 'var(--success)' : '#EF5350',
      preConfirm: () => {
        return {
          appeal_id: appealId,
          decision: decision,
          admin_notes: document.getElementById('appealNotes').value.trim()
        };
      }
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/appeals/review.php', result.value)
          .then(data => {
            if (data.success) {
              showToast(`Appeal ${decision}`, 'success');
              loadAppeals();
              loadAccounts();
            } else {
              showToast(data.message || 'Failed to review appeal', 'error');
            }
          }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  };

  // ===== HELPERS =====
  function escapeHtml(text) {
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.textContent = text || '';
    return div.innerHTML;
  }

  function formatDate(d) {
    if (!d) return '—';
    return new Date(d).toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month:'short', day:'numeric', year:'numeric' })
      + ' ' + new Date(d).toLocaleTimeString('en-US', { hour:'2-digit', minute:'2-digit' });
  }

  function renderPagination(total, page, perPage, containerId, loadFunc) {
    const totalPages = Math.ceil(total / perPage);
    const container = document.getElementById(containerId);
    container.innerHTML = '';
    if (totalPages <= 1) return;

    const prev = document.createElement('button');
    prev.className = 'page-btn'; prev.textContent = 'Previous'; prev.disabled = page <= 1;
    prev.addEventListener('click', () => { currentPage--; loadFunc(); });
    container.appendChild(prev);

    for (let i = Math.max(1,page-2); i <= Math.min(totalPages,page+2); i++) {
      const pb = document.createElement('button');
      pb.className = `page-btn ${i===page?'active':''}`;
      pb.textContent = i;
      pb.addEventListener('click', () => { currentPage = i; loadFunc(); });
      container.appendChild(pb);
    }

    const next = document.createElement('button');
    next.className = 'page-btn'; next.textContent = 'Next'; next.disabled = page >= totalPages;
    next.addEventListener('click', () => { currentPage++; loadFunc(); });
    container.appendChild(next);

    const info = document.createElement('span');
    info.className = 'pagination-info';
    info.textContent = `Showing ${(page-1)*perPage+1}–${Math.min(page*perPage,total)} of ${total}`;
    container.appendChild(info);
  }

});
```

---

### 3. `staff/manage_orders.php`

This is the staff's primary operational page — the most complex page in the staff role.

**PHP Logic:**
```
1. Include auth_check.php, require_role([ROLE_STAFF])
2. Check for ?highlight= query param (from dashboard redirect after confirming)
3. Include header.php, sidebar.php
```

**HTML Structure:**
```html
<div class="main-content">
  <div class="page-header">
    <h1>Manage Orders</h1>
    <p class="text-muted">Confirm, assign, and manage all customer orders.</p>
  </div>

  <!-- Filter Bar -->
  <div class="filter-bar" id="orderFilters">
    <button class="filter-btn active" data-filter="all">All Active</button>
    <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="pending">Pending</button>
    <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="confirmed">Confirmed</button>
    <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="assigned">Assigned</button>
    <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="on_delivery">On Delivery</button>
    <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="ready_for_pickup">Ready for Pickup</button>
  </div>

  <!-- Search -->
  <div class="toolbar-row">
    <div class="search-bar">
      <span class="material-icons search-icon">search</span>
      <input type="text" id="orderSearch" class="search-input" placeholder="Search by Order ID, customer name...">
    </div>
  </div>

  <!-- Bulk Actions Bar -->
  <div class="bulk-actions-bar" id="bulkActions" style="display:none;">
    <span id="bulkSelectedCount">0</span> order(s) selected
    <button class="btn btn-success btn-sm" id="bulkConfirmBtn">
      <span class="material-icons">check_circle</span> Confirm All
    </button>
    <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" id="bulkAssignAutoBtn">
      <span class="material-icons">person_add</span> Auto-Assign All
    </button>
    <button class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" id="bulkCancelBtn">
      <span class="material-icons">cancel</span> Cancel All
    </button>
  </div>

  <!-- Orders Table -->
  <div class="data-table-wrapper">
    <table class="data-table" id="ordersTable">
      <thead>
        <tr>
          <th><input type="checkbox" class="custom-checkbox" id="selectAllOrders"></th>
          <th>Order ID</th>
          <th>Customer Details</th>
          <th>Items</th>
          <th>Total Qty</th>
          <th>Payment</th>
          <th>Type</th>
          <th>Order Date</th>
          <th>Expected Delivery</th>
          <th>Rider</th>
          <th>Status</th>
          <th>Staff Comment</th>
          <th>Actions</th>
        </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody id="ordersBody">
        <tr class="loading-row"><td colspan="13"><div class="spinner"></div></td></tr>
      </tbody>
    </table>
  </div>

  <div class="pagination" id="ordersPagination"></div>

  <div class="empty-state" id="emptyOrders" style="display:none;">
    <span class="material-icons">inbox</span>
    <p>No orders found matching your criteria.</p>
  </div>
</div>
```

### `staff/css/manage_orders.css`

```
.toolbar-row:
  - Flex row, margin-bottom 16px

.bulk-actions-bar:
  - Glass card, flex row, align center, gap 12px, flex wrap
  - Padding: 12px 20px
  - Margin-bottom: 16px

.data-table:
  - Customer Details cell:
    .customer-details-cell: min-width 180px
    strong: customer name on first line
    phone: second line with phone icon
    address: third line with location icon, muted, smaller font, word-break
  - Items cell: each item on own line with icon, max-height 80px, overflow hidden, expand on hover or show "+X more"
  - Rider cell: show rider name or "Unassigned" in muted italic
  - Staff Comment cell: max-width 150px, truncated, title tooltip
  - Actions cell: nowrap, flex row, gap 4px

  - Grouped rows (same customer, same status):
    .order-group-header: slightly darker background, cursor pointer, expandable
      Shows: customer name, "X orders", combined status badge
      Click to expand/collapse individual orders underneath
    .order-group-children: hidden by default, shown when group is expanded
      Each child row is slightly indented (padding-left on first cell)

  - Highlighted row (from ?highlight= param):
    tr.highlight: box-shadow inset 3px 0 0 var(--primary), background slight primary tint
    Auto-scroll to highlighted row on page load

Responsive:
  @media (max-width: 768px):
    - Table horizontal scroll
    - bulk-actions-bar: flex wrap
    - Actions buttons stack or show fewer
```

### `staff/js/manage_orders.js`

```javascript
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {

  let currentFilter = 'all';
  let currentPage = 1;
  let searchText = '';
  const perPage = 50;
  const highlightOrderId = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search).get('highlight');

  loadOrders();

  // ===== FILTERS =====
  document.querySelectorAll('#orderFilters .filter-btn').forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      document.querySelectorAll('#orderFilters .filter-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
      this.classList.add('active');
      currentFilter = this.dataset.filter;
      currentPage = 1;
      loadOrders();
    });
  });

  // ===== SEARCH =====
  let searchTimeout;
  document.getElementById('orderSearch').addEventListener('input', function() {
    clearTimeout(searchTimeout);
    searchTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
      searchText = this.value.trim();
      currentPage = 1;
      loadOrders();
    }, 300);
  });

  // ===== LOAD ORDERS =====
  function loadOrders() {
    const activeStatuses = 'pending,confirmed,assigned,on_delivery,ready_for_pickup';
    const statusParam = currentFilter === 'all' ? activeStatuses : currentFilter;

    const params = {
      status: statusParam,
      search: searchText,
      page: currentPage,
      scope: 'manage'
    };

    document.getElementById('ordersBody').innerHTML =
      '<tr class="loading-row"><td colspan="13"><div class="spinner"></div></td></tr>';
    document.getElementById('emptyOrders').style.display = 'none';

    ajaxGet('/api/orders/get_orders.php', params)
      .then(data => {
        if (!data.orders || data.orders.length === 0) {
          document.getElementById('ordersBody').innerHTML = '';
          document.getElementById('emptyOrders').style.display = 'flex';
          document.getElementById('ordersPagination').innerHTML = '';
          return;
        }
        document.getElementById('emptyOrders').style.display = 'none';
        renderOrders(data.orders);
        renderPagination(data.total, data.page, data.per_page);

        // Highlight and scroll to order if specified
        if (highlightOrderId) {
          const highlightRow = document.querySelector(`tr[data-order-id="${highlightOrderId}"]`);
          if (highlightRow) {
            highlightRow.classList.add('highlight');
            highlightRow.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
          }
        }
      })
      .catch(() => showToast('Failed to load orders', 'error'));
  }

  // ===== RENDER ORDERS =====
  function renderOrders(orders) {
    const tbody = document.getElementById('ordersBody');
    tbody.innerHTML = '';

    const paymentLabels = { cod: 'Cash on Delivery', pickup: 'Pickup at Store', online: 'Online' };
    const typeLabels = { delivery: 'Delivery', pickup: 'Pickup' };

    // Group orders by customer + status for collapsing
    const groups = {};
    orders.forEach(order => {
      const key = `${order.customer_id}_${order.status}`;
      if (!groups[key]) groups[key] = [];
      groups[key].push(order);
    });

    Object.values(groups).forEach(group => {
      if (group.length > 1) {
        // Render group header (collapsible)
        renderGroupHeader(tbody, group);
        // Render individual orders (hidden initially)
        group.forEach(order => {
          renderOrderRow(tbody, order, paymentLabels, typeLabels, true); // isGroupChild = true
        });
      } else {
        // Single order — render normally
        renderOrderRow(tbody, group[0], paymentLabels, typeLabels, false);
      }
    });

    initCheckboxListeners();
  }

  function renderGroupHeader(tbody, group) {
    const first = group[0];
    const totalItems = group.reduce((sum, o) => sum + o.items.reduce((s, i) => s + parseInt(i.quantity), 0), 0);
    const groupId = `group_${first.customer_id}_${first.status}`;

    const tr = document.createElement('tr');
    tr.className = 'order-group-header';
    tr.dataset.groupId = groupId;
    tr.innerHTML = `
      <td><input type="checkbox" class="custom-checkbox group-checkbox" data-group-id="${groupId}"></td>
      <td colspan="2">
        <span class="material-icons group-toggle" style="vertical-align:middle;cursor:pointer;">expand_more</span>
        <strong>${escapeHtml(first.customer_name)}</strong>
        <span class="text-muted">(${group.length} orders)</span>
      </td>
      <td>${totalItems} items total</td>
      <td colspan="3"></td>
      <td colspan="2"></td>
      <td><span class="badge badge-${first.status.replace(/_/g,'-')}">${formatStatus(first.status)}</span></td>
      <td></td>
      <td class="actions-cell">
        ${getGroupActions(first.status, group.map(o => o.id))}
      </td>
    `;

    tr.querySelector('.group-toggle').addEventListener('click', function() {
      const children = tbody.querySelectorAll(`.group-child[data-group-id="${groupId}"]`);
      const isExpanded = this.textContent === 'expand_less';
      children.forEach(c => c.style.display = isExpanded ? 'none' : '');
      this.textContent = isExpanded ? 'expand_more' : 'expand_less';
    });

    tbody.appendChild(tr);
  }

  function getGroupActions(status, orderIds) {
    const idsJson = JSON.stringify(orderIds);
    let html = '';
    if (status === 'pending') {
      html = `<button class="btn btn-sm btn-success" onclick='bulkActionGroup(${idsJson}, "confirm")'>Confirm All</button>`;
    } else if (status === 'confirmed') {
      html = `<button class="btn btn-sm btn-primary" onclick='bulkActionGroup(${idsJson}, "assign_auto")'>Auto-Assign All</button>`;
    }
    html += ` <button class="btn btn-sm btn-danger" onclick='bulkActionGroup(${idsJson}, "cancel")'>Cancel All</button>`;
    return html;
  }

  function renderOrderRow(tbody, order, paymentLabels, typeLabels, isGroupChild) {
    const tr = document.createElement('tr');
    tr.dataset.orderId = order.id;
    tr.dataset.status = order.status;
    if (isGroupChild) {
      tr.className = 'group-child';
      tr.dataset.groupId = `group_${order.customer_id}_${order.status}`;
      tr.style.display = 'none'; // Hidden by default, expand via group header
    }

    const itemsHtml = order.items.map(i =>
      `<span class="item-with-icon"><img src="${i.item_icon || '/assets/images/default-item.png'}" class="item-icon-sm">${escapeHtml(i.item_name)} (×${i.quantity})</span>`
    ).join('<br>');

    const totalQty = order.items.reduce((s, i) => s + parseInt(i.quantity), 0);

    const customerDetails = `
      <strong>${escapeHtml(order.customer_name)}</strong>
      <span class="customer-phone"><span class="material-icons" style="font-size:14px;vertical-align:middle;">phone</span> ${escapeHtml(order.customer_phone || 'N/A')}</span>
      <small class="customer-address"><span class="material-icons" style="font-size:14px;vertical-align:middle;">location_on</span> ${escapeHtml(order.delivery_address || order.customer_default_address || 'N/A')}</small>
    `;

    tr.innerHTML = `
      <td><input type="checkbox" class="custom-checkbox order-checkbox" data-order-id="${order.id}"></td>
      <td><strong>#${order.id}</strong></td>
      <td class="customer-details-cell">${customerDetails}</td>
      <td class="items-cell">${itemsHtml}</td>
      <td>${totalQty}</td>
      <td>${paymentLabels[order.payment_type] || order.payment_type}</td>
      <td>${typeLabels[order.delivery_type] || order.delivery_type}</td>
      <td>${formatDate(order.order_date)}</td>
      <td>${order.expected_delivery_date ? formatDate(order.expected_delivery_date) : '<span class="text-muted">—</span>'}</td>
      <td>${order.rider_name || '<span class="text-muted italic">Unassigned</span>'}</td>
      <td><span class="badge badge-${order.status.replace(/_/g,'-')}">${formatStatus(order.status)}</span></td>
      <td class="truncate-cell" title="${escapeHtml(order.staff_comment || '')}">${order.staff_comment || '<span class="text-muted">—</span>'}</td>
      <td class="actions-cell">${getOrderActions(order)}</td>
    `;

    tbody.appendChild(tr);
  }

  // ===== ORDER ACTIONS BY STATUS =====
  function getOrderActions(order) {
    let html = '';

    switch(order.status) {
      case 'pending':
        html = `
          <button class="btn-icon btn-success" title="Confirm" onclick="confirmOrder(${order.id})">
            <span class="material-icons">check_circle</span>
          </button>
          <button class="btn-icon btn-danger" title="Cancel" onclick="cancelOrder(${order.id})">
            <span class="material-icons">cancel</span>
          </button>
        `;
        break;

      case 'confirmed':
        if (order.delivery_type === 'delivery') {
          html = `
            <button class="btn-icon btn-primary" title="Assign Rider" onclick="assignRider(${order.id})">
              <span class="material-icons">person_add</span>
            </button>
          `;
        }
        if (order.delivery_type === 'pickup') {
          html += `
            <button class="btn-icon btn-info" title="Ready for Pickup" onclick="markReadyForPickup(${order.id})">
              <span class="material-icons">store</span>
            </button>
          `;
        }
        html += `
          <button class="btn-icon btn-danger" title="Cancel" onclick="cancelOrder(${order.id})">
            <span class="material-icons">cancel</span>
          </button>
        `;
        break;

      case 'assigned':
        html = `
          <button class="btn-icon btn-primary" title="Reassign Rider" onclick="assignRider(${order.id})">
            <span class="material-icons">swap_horiz</span>
          </button>
          <button class="btn-icon btn-danger" title="Cancel" onclick="cancelOrder(${order.id})">
            <span class="material-icons">cancel</span>
          </button>
        `;
        break;

      case 'on_delivery':
        html = `
          <button class="btn-icon btn-info" title="Update Status" onclick="updateOrderStatus(${order.id})">
            <span class="material-icons">edit</span>
          </button>
          <button class="btn-icon btn-danger" title="Cancel" onclick="cancelOrder(${order.id})">
            <span class="material-icons">cancel</span>
          </button>
        `;
        break;

      case 'ready_for_pickup':
        html = `
          <button class="btn-icon btn-success" title="Mark Picked Up" onclick="markPickedUp(${order.id})">
            <span class="material-icons">shopping_bag</span>
          </button>
          <button class="btn-icon btn-danger" title="Cancel" onclick="cancelOrder(${order.id})">
            <span class="material-icons">cancel</span>
          </button>
        `;
        break;
    }

    // Add comment button for all active orders
    html += `
      <button class="btn-icon btn-outline" title="Add Comment" onclick="addComment(${order.id})">
        <span class="material-icons">comment</span>
      </button>
    `;

    return html;
  }

  // ===== CONFIRM ORDER =====
  window.confirmOrder = function(orderId) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Confirm Order #' + orderId + '?',
      html: '<p>Stock will be decremented for all items.</p>',
      icon: 'question',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Confirm Order',
      confirmButtonColor: 'var(--success)'
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/orders/update_status.php', {
          order_id: orderId,
          new_status: 'confirmed'
        }).then(data => {
          if (data.success) {
            // Ask to assign rider
            Swal.fire({
              title: 'Order Confirmed!',
              text: 'Assign a rider now?',
              icon: 'success',
              showDenyButton: true,
              showCancelButton: false,
              confirmButtonText: 'Yes, Assign',
              denyButtonText: 'Later',
              confirmButtonColor: 'var(--primary)'
            }).then(r => {
              if (r.isConfirmed) {
                assignRider(orderId);
              } else {
                loadOrders();
              }
            });
          } else {
            showToast(data.message || 'Failed to confirm', 'error');
          }
        }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  };

  // ===== ASSIGN RIDER =====
  window.assignRider = function(orderId) {
    // First fetch available riders
    ajaxGet('/api/riders/get_available.php')
      .then(data => {
        if (!data.riders || data.riders.length === 0) {
          Swal.fire({
            title: 'No Riders Available',
            html: `
              <p>There are currently no available riders.</p>
              <p style="margin-top:8px;color:var(--text-muted);">Would you like to add a comment for the customer?</p>
              <textarea id="noRiderComment" class="swal2-textarea" placeholder="e.g., Waiting for available rider" rows="2"></textarea>
            `,
            icon: 'warning',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonText: 'Save Comment',
            cancelButtonText: 'Close',
            confirmButtonColor: 'var(--primary)',
            preConfirm: () => {
              return document.getElementById('noRiderComment').value.trim();
            }
          }).then(r => {
            if (r.isConfirmed && r.value) {
              ajaxPost('/api/orders/update_status.php', {
                order_id: orderId,
                new_status: null, // Don't change status, just add comment
                comment: r.value
              }).then(() => loadOrders());
            }
          });
          return;
        }

        // Build rider selection list
        let riderListHtml = data.riders.map(r => `
          <div class="rider-select-item" data-rider-id="${r.rider_id}" onclick="selectRiderItem(this, ${r.rider_id})">
            <div class="rider-select-info">
              <strong>${escapeHtml(r.full_name)}</strong>
              <span class="text-muted">${r.current_load} active deliveries</span>
            </div>
            <span class="badge ${r.is_available ? 'badge-confirmed' : 'badge-cancelled'}">
              ${r.is_available ? 'Available' : 'Unavailable'}
            </span>
          </div>
        `).join('');

        Swal.fire({
          title: 'Assign Rider',
          html: `
            <div style="margin-bottom:16px;">
              <button class="btn btn-sm btn-primary" id="autoAssignBtn" style="width:100%;margin-bottom:12px;">
                <span class="material-icons" style="vertical-align:middle;">auto_fix_high</span>
                Auto-Assign (Least Loaded)
              </button>
            </div>
            <p style="font-weight:500;margin-bottom:8px;">Or select a rider:</p>
            <div class="rider-select-list" id="riderSelectList" style="max-height:300px;overflow-y:auto;">
              ${riderListHtml}
            </div>
            <input type="hidden" id="selectedRiderId" value="">
          `,
          showCancelButton: true,
          confirmButtonText: 'Assign Selected',
          cancelButtonText: 'Cancel',
          confirmButtonColor: 'var(--primary)',
          didOpen: () => {
            document.getElementById('autoAssignBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
              document.getElementById('selectedRiderId').value = 'auto';
              Swal.clickConfirm();
            });
          },
          preConfirm: () => {
            const riderId = document.getElementById('selectedRiderId').value;
            if (!riderId) {
              Swal.showValidationMessage('Please select a rider or use Auto-Assign');
              return false;
            }
            return riderId;
          }
        }).then(result => {
          if (result.isConfirmed) {
            ajaxPost('/api/orders/assign_rider.php', {
              order_id: orderId,
              rider_id: result.value
            }).then(data => {
              if (data.success) {
                showToast(data.message || 'Rider assigned!', 'success');
                loadOrders();
              } else {
                showToast(data.message || 'Failed to assign rider', 'error');
              }
            }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
          }
        });
      })
      .catch(() => showToast('Failed to load riders', 'error'));
  };

  // Rider selection helper
  window.selectRiderItem = function(element, riderId) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.rider-select-item').forEach(i => i.classList.remove('selected'));
    element.classList.add('selected');
    document.getElementById('selectedRiderId').value = riderId;
  };

  // ===== CANCEL ORDER =====
  window.cancelOrder = function(orderId) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Cancel Order #' + orderId + '?',
      html: `
        <p style="color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:12px;">
          Stock will be restored if the order was already confirmed.
        </p>
        <textarea id="cancelReason" class="swal2-textarea" placeholder="Reason for cancellation (required)" rows="3"></textarea>
      `,
      icon: 'warning',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Yes, Cancel Order',
      cancelButtonText: 'No, Keep It',
      confirmButtonColor: '#EF5350',
      preConfirm: () => {
        const reason = document.getElementById('cancelReason').value.trim();
        if (!reason) {
          Swal.showValidationMessage('Cancellation reason is required');
          return false;
        }
        return reason;
      }
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/orders/cancel_order.php', {
          order_id: orderId,
          reason: result.value
        }).then(data => {
          if (data.success) {
            showToast('Order cancelled', 'success');
            loadOrders();
          } else {
            showToast(data.message || 'Failed to cancel', 'error');
          }
        }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  };

  // ===== UPDATE ORDER STATUS (for on_delivery) =====
  window.updateOrderStatus = function(orderId) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Update Order #' + orderId,
      html: `
        <p style="margin-bottom:12px;">Select new status:</p>
        <select id="newStatusSelect" class="swal2-select" style="width:100%;">
          <option value="pending">Pending</option>
          <option value="confirmed">Confirmed</option>
          <option value="delivered">Delivered</option>
          <option value="ready_for_pickup">Ready for Pickup</option>
          <option value="picked_up">Picked Up</option>
        </select>
        <textarea id="statusComment" class="swal2-textarea" placeholder="Comment (optional)" rows="2" style="margin-top:12px;"></textarea>
      `,
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Update Status',
      confirmButtonColor: 'var(--primary)',
      preConfirm: () => {
        return {
          order_id: orderId,
          new_status: document.getElementById('newStatusSelect').value,
          comment: document.getElementById('statusComment').value.trim()
        };
      }
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/orders/update_status.php', result.value)
          .then(data => {
            if (data.success) {
              showToast('Status updated', 'success');
              loadOrders();
            } else {
              showToast(data.message || 'Failed to update', 'error');
            }
          }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  };

  // ===== READY FOR PICKUP =====
  window.markReadyForPickup = function(orderId) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Mark Ready for Pickup?',
      text: 'Order #' + orderId + ' will be marked as ready for the customer to collect.',
      icon: 'question',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Yes, Ready',
      confirmButtonColor: 'var(--info)'
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/orders/update_status.php', {
          order_id: orderId,
          new_status: 'ready_for_pickup'
        }).then(data => {
          if (data.success) {
            showToast('Order marked as Ready for Pickup', 'success');
            loadOrders();
          } else {
            showToast(data.message || 'Failed', 'error');
          }
        }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  };

  // ===== MARK PICKED UP =====
  window.markPickedUp = function(orderId) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Mark as Picked Up?',
      text: 'Confirm the customer has collected Order #' + orderId + '.',
      icon: 'question',
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Yes, Picked Up',
      confirmButtonColor: 'var(--success)'
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/orders/update_status.php', {
          order_id: orderId,
          new_status: 'picked_up'
        }).then(data => {
          if (data.success) {
            showToast('Order marked as Picked Up', 'success');
            loadOrders();
          } else {
            showToast(data.message || 'Failed', 'error');
          }
        }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  };

  // ===== ADD COMMENT =====
  window.addComment = function(orderId) {
    Swal.fire({
      title: 'Staff Comment',
      html: `
        <p style="color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:8px;font-size:0.9em;">This comment is visible to the customer.</p>
        <textarea id="staffComment" class="swal2-textarea" placeholder="e.g., Waiting for available rider..." rows="3"></textarea>
      `,
      showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Save Comment',
      confirmButtonColor: 'var(--primary)',
      preConfirm: () => document.getElementById('staffComment').value.trim()
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/orders/update_status.php', {
          order_id: orderId,
          comment: result.value
        }).then(data => {
          if (data.success) {
            showToast('Comment saved', 'success');
            loadOrders();
          } else {
            showToast(data.message || 'Failed', 'error');
          }
        }).catch(() => showToast('An error occurred', 'error'));
      }
    });
  };

  // ===== BULK GROUP ACTION =====
  window.bulkActionGroup = function(orderIds, action) {
    if (action === 'cancel') {
      Swal.fire({
        title: `Cancel ${orderIds.length} Orders?`,
        html: '<textarea id="bulkReason" class="swal2-textarea" placeholder="Reason (required)" rows="3"></textarea>',
        icon: 'warning', showCancelButton: true,
        confirmButtonText: 'Cancel All', confirmButtonColor: '#EF5350',
        preConfirm: () => {
          const r = document.getElementById('bulkReason').value.trim();
          if (!r) { Swal.showValidationMessage('Reason required'); return false; }
          return r;
        }
      }).then(result => {
        if (result.isConfirmed) {
          ajaxPost('/api/orders/bulk_update.php', {
            order_ids: JSON.stringify(orderIds), action: 'cancel', reason: result.value
          }).then(d => { showToast(`${d.success||0} cancelled`, 'success'); loadOrders(); })
            .catch(() => showToast('Error', 'error'));
        }
      });
    } else {
      ajaxPost('/api/orders/bulk_update.php', {
        order_ids: JSON.stringify(orderIds), action: action
      }).then(d => { showToast(`${d.success||0} updated`, 'success'); loadOrders(); })
        .catch(() => showToast('Error', 'error'));
    }
  };

  // ===== BULK ACTIONS (from toolbar) =====
  document.getElementById('bulkConfirmBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
    const ids = getSelectedOrderIds();
    if (!ids.length) return;
    ajaxPost('/api/orders/bulk_update.php', { order_ids: JSON.stringify(ids), action: 'confirm' })
      .then(d => { showToast(`${d.success||0} confirmed`, 'success'); loadOrders(); })
      .catch(() => showToast('Error', 'error'));
  });

  document.getElementById('bulkAssignAutoBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
    const ids = getSelectedOrderIds();
    if (!ids.length) return;
    ajaxPost('/api/orders/bulk_update.php', { order_ids: JSON.stringify(ids), action: 'assign_auto' })
      .then(d => {
        showToast(`${d.success||0} assigned`, 'success');
        if (d.failed > 0) showToast(`${d.failed} could not be assigned (no riders?)`, 'warning');
        loadOrders();
      }).catch(() => showToast('Error', 'error'));
  });

  document.getElementById('bulkCancelBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
    const ids = getSelectedOrderIds();
    if (!ids.length) return;
    Swal.fire({
      title: `Cancel ${ids.length} Order(s)?`,
      html: '<textarea id="bulkCancelReason" class="swal2-textarea" placeholder="Reason (required)" rows="3"></textarea>',
      icon: 'warning', showCancelButton: true,
      confirmButtonText: 'Cancel All', confirmButtonColor: '#EF5350',
      preConfirm: () => {
        const r = document.getElementById('bulkCancelReason').value.trim();
        if (!r) { Swal.showValidationMessage('Reason required'); return false; }
        return r;
      }
    }).then(result => {
      if (result.isConfirmed) {
        ajaxPost('/api/orders/bulk_update.php', {
          order_ids: JSON.stringify(ids), action: 'cancel', reason: result.value
        }).then(d => { showToast(`${d.success||0} cancelled`, 'success'); loadOrders(); })
          .catch(() => showToast('Error', 'error'));
      }
    });
  });

  // ===== CHECKBOX HANDLING =====
  function initCheckboxListeners() {
    document.getElementById('selectAllOrders').addEventListener('change', function() {
      document.querySelectorAll('.order-checkbox').forEach(cb => { cb.checked = this.checked; });
      updateBulkBar();
    });
  }

  document.getElementById('ordersBody').addEventListener('change', function(e) {
    if (e.target.classList.contains('order-checkbox') || e.target.classList.contains('group-checkbox')) {
      updateBulkBar();
    }
  });

  function updateBulkBar() {
    const checked = document.querySelectorAll('.order-checkbox:checked').length;
    document.getElementById('bulkActions').style.display = checked > 0 ? 'flex' : 'none';
    document.getElementById('bulkSelectedCount').textContent = checked;
  }

  function getSelectedOrderIds() {
    const ids = [];
    document.querySelectorAll('.order-checkbox:checked').forEach(cb => ids.push(parseInt(cb.dataset.orderId)));
    return ids;
  }

  // ===== HELPERS =====
  function formatStatus(s) {
    const l = { pending:'Pending', confirmed:'Confirmed', assigned:'Assigned', on_delivery:'On Delivery', delivered:'Delivered', accepted:'Accepted', ready_for_pickup:'Ready for Pickup', picked_up:'Picked Up', cancelled:'Cancelled' };
    return l[s] || s;
  }
  function formatDate(d) {
    if (!d) return '—';
    return new Date(d).toLocaleDateString('en-US',{month:'short',day:'numeric',year:'numeric'}) + ' ' + new Date(d).toLocaleTimeString('en-US',{hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'});
  }
  function escapeHtml(t) { const d = document.createElement('div'); d.textContent = t||''; return d.innerHTML; }

  function renderPagination(total, page, perPage) {
    const totalPages = Math.ceil(total / perPage);
    const container = document.getElementById('ordersPagination');
    container.innerHTML = '';
    if (totalPages <= 1) return;
    const prev = document.createElement('button'); prev.className='page-btn'; prev.textContent='Previous'; prev.disabled=page<=1;
    prev.addEventListener('click', () => { currentPage--; loadOrders(); }); container.appendChild(prev);
    for (let i=Math.max(1,page-2); i<=Math.min(totalPages,page+2); i++) {
      const pb = document.createElement('button'); pb.className=`page-btn ${i===page?'active':''}`; pb.textContent=i;
      pb.addEventListener('click', () => { currentPage=i; loadOrders(); }); container.appendChild(pb);
    }
    const next = document.createElement('button'); next.className='page-btn'; next.textContent='Next'; next.disabled=page>=totalPages;
    next.addEventListener('click', () => { currentPage++; loadOrders(); }); container.appendChild(next);
    const info = document.createElement('span'); info.className='pagination-info';
    info.textContent = `Showing ${(page-1)*perPage+1}–${Math.min(page*perPage,total)} of ${total}`;
    container.appendChild(info);
  }

});
```

### 4. `staff/order_history.php`

**PHP Logic:** Include auth_check, require_role([ROLE_STAFF]), include header/sidebar. Data loaded via AJAX.

**HTML Structure:** Same pattern as customer order history but showing ALL orders (not just own). Staff sees all customers' order history.

```html
<div class="main-content">
  <div class="page-header">
    <h1>Order History</h1>
    <p class="text-muted">View all completed and cancelled orders.</p>

  <div class="toolbar">
    <div class="filter-bar" id="historyFilters">
      <button class="filter-btn active" data-filter="all">All</button>

      <button class="filter-btn" data-filter="picked_up">Picked Up</button>

    <div class="toolbar-right">
      <div class="search-bar">
        <span class="material-icons search-icon">search</span>
        <input type="text" id="historySearch" class="search-input" placeholder="Search Order ID, customer, item...">
      </div>
      <div class="date-range">
        <input type="date" id="dateFrom" class="float-input">
        <span class="text-muted">to</span>
        <input type="date" id="dateTo" class="float-input">
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

  <div class="data-table-wrapper">
    <table class="data-table" id="historyTable">
      <thead>
        <tr>
          <th>Order ID</th>
          <th>Customer</th>
          <th>Items</th>
          <th>Total Qty</th>
          <th>Payment</th>
          <th>Delivery Type</th>
          <th>Status</th>
          <th>Total Amount</th>
          <th>Rider</th>
          <th>Order Date</th>
          <th>Delivered Date</th>
          <th>Cancel Reason</th>
          <th>Cancelled By</th>
          <th>Customer Confirmed</th>
        </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody id="historyBody">
        <tr class="loading-row"><td colspan="14"><div class="spinner"></div></td></tr>
      </tbody>
    </table>
  </div>

  <div class="pagination" id="historyPagination"></div>
  <div class="empty-state" id="emptyHistory" style="display:none;">
    <span class="material-icons">history</span>
    <p>No order history found.</p>
  </div>
</div>
```

### `staff/css/order_history.css` and `staff/js/order_history.js`

Follow the same pattern as customer's `order_history.css/js` but:
- Shows ALL orders (not filtered by customer_id)
- Table has columns: Order ID, Customer (name), Items, Total Qty, Payment, Delivery Type, Status, Total Amount, Rider, Order Date, Delivered Date, Cancel Reason (truncated), Cancelled By (shows role+name), Customer Confirmed (Yes/No/—)
- Same filters, search, date range, pagination pattern
- No "Reorder" button (staff doesn't place orders)
- No "View Receipt" button (optional — can include for reference)

### `staff/css/inventory.css`

```
- Item column: flex row, icon + name. Icon: 40x40px, rounded
- Stock count: bold. If below low_stock_threshold: red color + warning icon
- Price: formatted with peso sign
- Status: badge (active=green, inactive=grey, out_of_stock=red)
- Low Stock column: warning triangle icon if stock <= threshold, otherwise "OK" in green
- No action buttons (read-only)
```

### `staff/js/inventory.js`

Load inventory items via `ajaxGet('/api/inventory/get_items.php')`, render read-only table with search and pagination. No edit/delete/add buttons. Show low stock threshold from settings. Items below threshold get a warning icon and highlighted row.

### 6. `staff/rider_statistics.php`

**PHP Logic:** Include auth_check, require_role([ROLE_STAFF]). Data loaded via AJAX.

**HTML Structure:**
```html
<div class="main-content">
  <div class="page-header">
    <h1>Rider Statistics</h1>
    <p class="text-muted">Monitor rider performance and availability.</p>
  </div>

  <!-- Stats Cards -->
  <div class="stats-grid two-cols">
    <div class="stat-card">
      <div class="stat-icon" style="background:var(--purple)">
        <span class="material-icons">delivery_dining</span>
      </div>
      <div class="stat-info">
        <span class="stat-number" id="totalRiders">—</span>
        <span class="stat-label">Total Riders</span>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="stat-card">
      <div class="stat-icon" style="background:var(--success)">
        <span class="material-icons">how_to_reg</span>
      </div>
      <div class="stat-info">
        <span class="stat-number" id="availableRiders">—</span>
        <span class="stat-label">Available Riders</span>
```

### `staff/css/rider_statistics.css`

```
.stats-grid.two-cols:
  - Grid: 2 columns desktop, 1 mobile
  - Gap 20px, margin-bottom 24px

- Rank column: priority-number circle (1,2,3 in colored circles — gold/silver/bronze for top 3, grey for rest)
- Current Status column: badge — "Available" (green), "Unavailable" (grey/red), "On Delivery" (teal)
- Success Rate: percentage with subtle progress bar behind text
- Completed: bold number, green tint
- Pending: number, orange tint if > 0
```

### `staff/js/rider_statistics.js`

```javascript
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {

  loadRiderStats();

  function loadRiderStats() {
    ajaxGet('/api/riders/get_statistics.php')
      .then(data => {
        document.getElementById('totalRiders').textContent = data.total_riders || 0;
        document.getElementById('availableRiders').textContent = data.available_riders || 0;
        renderRiders(data.riders || []);
      })
      .catch(() => showToast('Failed to load rider statistics', 'error'));
  }

  function renderRiders(riders) {
    const tbody = document.getElementById('ridersBody');
    tbody.innerHTML = '';

    if (riders.length === 0) {
      tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="8" class="text-center text-muted">No riders found</td></tr>';
      return;
    }

    riders.forEach((rider, index) => {
      const rank = index + 1;
      const rankClass = rank <= 3 ? `rank-${rank}` : 'rank-default';

      // Determine status display
      let statusHtml = '';
      if (rider.on_delivery_count > 0) {
        statusHtml = '<span class="badge badge-on-delivery">On Delivery</span>';
      } else if (rider.is_available) {
        statusHtml = '<span class="badge badge-confirmed">Available</span>';
      } else {
        statusHtml = '<span class="badge badge-cancelled">Unavailable</span>';
      }

      const successRate = rider.completed > 0
        ? ((rider.completed / (rider.completed + rider.cancelled)) * 100).toFixed(1)
        : '0.0';

      const tr = document.createElement('tr');
      tr.innerHTML = `
        <td><span class="rank-number ${rankClass}">${rank}</span></td>
        <td><strong>${escapeHtml(rider.full_name)}</strong></td>
        <td>${escapeHtml(rider.email)}</td>
        <td>${statusHtml}</td>
        <td><strong class="text-success">${rider.completed}</strong></td>
        <td>${rider.pending > 0 ? `<strong class="text-warning">${rider.pending}</strong>` : '0'}</td>
        <td>
          <div class="success-rate-cell">
            <div class="success-rate-bar" style="width:${successRate}%"></div>
            <span>${successRate}%</span>
          </div>
        </td>
        <td>
          <button class="btn-icon btn-info" title="Show Full Info" onclick="showRiderInfo(${rider.rider_id})">
            <span class="material-icons">info</span>
          </button>
        </td>
      `;
      tbody.appendChild(tr);
    });
  }

  // Show Rider Full Info
  window.showRiderInfo = function(riderId) {
    ajaxGet('/api/accounts/get_accounts.php', { user_id: riderId })
      .then(data => {
        const r = data.account || data.accounts?.find(a => a.id === riderId);
        if (!r) { showToast('Rider not found', 'error'); return; }

        Swal.fire({
          title: 'Rider Information',
          html: `
            <div style="text-align:left;line-height:2;">
              <p><strong>Full Name:</strong> ${escapeHtml(r.full_name)}</p>
              <p><strong>Username:</strong> ${escapeHtml(r.username)}</p>
              <p><strong>Email:</strong> ${escapeHtml(r.email)}</p>
              <p><strong>Phone:</strong> ${escapeHtml(r.phone)}</p>
              <p><strong>Status:</strong> <span class="badge badge-${r.status}">${r.status}</span></p>
              <p><strong>Available:</strong> ${r.is_available ? 'Yes' : 'No'}</p>
              <p><strong>Member Since:</strong> ${formatDate(r.created_at)}</p>
            </div>
          `,
          confirmButtonText: 'Close',
          confirmButtonColor: 'var(--primary)'
        });
      }).catch(() => showToast('Failed to load rider info', 'error'));
  };

  function escapeHtml(t) { const d=document.createElement('div'); d.textContent=t||''; return d.innerHTML; }
  function formatDate(d) { if(!d) return '—'; return new Date(d).toLocaleDateString('en-US',{month:'short',day:'numeric',year:'numeric'}); }

});
```

---

### 7. `staff/settings.php`

**PHP Logic:** Include auth_check, require_role([ROLE_STAFF]). Fetch own user data fresh from DB. Include header/sidebar.

**HTML Structure:** Same as rider settings — Profile section (Full Name, Username disabled, Email, Phone) + Password section. No addresses, no appeals, no availability toggle, no system settings. Staff can only manage their own profile and password.

### `staff/css/settings.css`

Same layout as rider settings.css — `.settings-section`, `.form-grid`, account info display.

### `staff/js/settings.js`

Same as rider settings.js — Profile form submit via `ajaxPost('/api/settings/update_profile.php')`, Password form submit via `ajaxPost('/api/settings/change_password.php')`. Same validation rules.

## IMPORTANT IMPLEMENTATION NOTES FOR STAFF PAGES

1. **Staff CANNOT see Staff/Admin/Super Admin accounts** in Account Management. The `api/accounts/get_accounts.php` endpoint filters by role when the caller is `staff` — only returning `customer` and `rider` accounts. The frontend should never attempt to display or modify higher-role accounts.

2. **Staff CANNOT create Staff/Admin accounts.** The "Add Account" dialog only offers `Customer` and `Rider` as role options. The API enforces this restriction.

3. **Order grouping in Manage Orders:** When multiple orders exist from the same customer with the same status, they should be grouped into a collapsible row. The group header shows customer name, order count, and combined actions. Clicking the expand arrow reveals individual orders. Individual orders within a group are indented slightly. Actions on the group header apply to ALL orders in the group.

4. **Rider assignment dialog** shows a list of available riders with their current delivery load (number of assigned + on_delivery orders). Staff can select a specific rider or click "Auto-Assign" which selects the least-loaded available rider. If no riders are available, staff is offered the option to add a comment to the order explaining the delay.

5. **Staff can cancel orders at ANY status** but must always provide a reason. The cancellation record includes who cancelled it (staff's user_id). Stock is restored automatically for orders that were already confirmed.

6. **Inventory page is READ-ONLY.** No add, edit, restock, or delete buttons. The table shows current stock levels, prices, and status. Items below the `low_stock_threshold` setting are highlighted with a warning icon. This helps staff make informed decisions when confirming orders.

7. **Rider Statistics page** shows all riders ranked by completed deliveries. Each rider shows: name, email, current status (Available/Unavailable/On Delivery), completed count, pending count, and success rate. The "Show Info" button shows a dialog with full rider details (no password).

8. **Cancellation Appeals** are shown in the Account Management page below the accounts table. Staff can approve (unflag customer, reset cancellation count) or deny (keep flagged, add admin notes) appeals.

9. **All tables render max 50 items per page** with pagination.

10. **Every AJAX call** uses `ajaxPost()`/`ajaxGet()` from `global.js` with automatic CSRF token attachment and `.catch()` error handling.

11. **Dark mode support** via CSS variables only — never hardcode colors in page-specific CSS.

12. **All date/time** formatted for Philippines Manila timezone.

13. **Glass card effect** used for: stat cards, preview sections, settings sections, rider statistics table wrapper. Subtle, not overused.

14. **Staff settings page** is simple: Profile (cannot change username) + Password change. No system settings, no addresses, no appeals, no availability.

15. **The `rider-select-item` class** used in the assign rider dialog needs CSS styling:
```css
.rider-select-item {
  display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center;
  padding: 12px 16px; border: 1px solid var(--border); border-radius: var(--radius-sm);
  margin-bottom: 8px; cursor: pointer; transition: var(--transition);
}
.rider-select-item:hover { background: var(--surface); }
.rider-select-item.selected { border-color: var(--primary); background: rgba(21,101,192,0.05); }
.rider-select-info { display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 2px; }
```
Add this to `manage_orders.css`.

16. **Success rate bar** in rider statistics:
```css
.success-rate-cell { position: relative; min-width: 80px; }
.success-rate-bar { position: absolute; left: 0; top: 0; bottom: 0; background: var(--success); opacity: 0.15; border-radius: var(--radius-sm); }
.success-rate-cell span { position: relative; z-index: 1; font-weight: 600; }
```
Add this to `rider_statistics.css`.

17. **Rank circles** for rider statistics:
```css
.rank-number { display: inline-flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center;
  width: 28px; height: 28px; border-radius: 50%; font-weight: 700; font-size: 0.85em; color: white; }
.rank-1 { background: #FFD700; } /* Gold */
.rank-2 { background: #C0C0C0; } /* Silver */
.rank-3 { background: #CD7F32; } /* Bronze */
.rank-default { background: var(--text-muted); }
```
Add this to `rider_statistics.css`.
